International Commercial Telegrams 56

—Special Commercial Telegram from Reuters, March 20th—

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price: Today's London gold price is 136 shillings and 2 pence, down 4 pence from yesterday's price.

London Silver: The London silver market was firm this morning. The spot price is 20 pence 1875, and the futures price is 20 pence 25, both up 3125. India and speculators bought in the morning, with some selling. The market closed steady.

New York Silver: The silver market is trending higher because of the passage of the Steagall Amendment and firm news from abroad. People's sentiment is tending towards the bullish side, awaiting new developments in Washington. The bullish trend can still be maintained, and the future looks even better because the silver faction members in Washington are very active, and it is expected that both the House and Senate will pass some silver legislation.

Bombay Silver: The Bombay silver market closed quietly today. The spot price fell 1 anna to 55 rupees and 10 annas. Futures all fell 2 pounds.

Exchange Rates: British-American Exchange: Today's London foreign exchange market was quite stable. The British-American exchange rate opened at $5.01375, which was 375 higher than yesterday's British-American exchange rate close. Later, it fell 4375, but the price soon rose again. The final exchange rate was $5.011875, which was 1875 lower than the opening price.

British-French Exchange: The opening price was 77 francs 56, which was 6 pounds higher than yesterday's price, and then fell 10 pounds. It then returned to 77 francs 53.

American-British Exchange Rate: New York's closing exchange rate for British pounds on the previous day was 5.1050. Today's opening price was 5.25, the second trade was 5.09625, the third trade was 5.1075, the fourth trade was 5.11, the fifth trade was 5.10875, and the sixth trade was 5.11.

American-French Exchange Rate: New York's exchange rate for French francs was 6.5850.

Cotton and Wheat: New York Cotton: Sentiment in the cotton market is mixed. At the opening, brokers and those in New Orleans and the Far East were buying, while short sellers were also covering, so after the price rose slightly, the market stabilized. The ginning report did not disturb the cotton market.

Bombay Cotton: The Bombay cotton market was quiet today. Bulls were taking some profits. The April-May term price for White Broach cotton was 199 rupees and a half, down 2 rupees and a half.

Liverpool Cotton: Liverpool cotton was slightly softer today. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, the May term price was 6.16, down 1 pound.

Liverpool Wheat: The Liverpool wheat May term price rose 375 to 4 shillings and 3 pence.

Rubber: London: The rubber market was firm today. The April-June term price was 5 shillings and 32/3, the same as yesterday's price.

New York: The rubber market opened steadily because non-official sources denied that the restriction negotiations had reached a standstill.

Securities: New York: The securities market opened unevenly today. Operators are very concerned about the outcome of labor disputes in the automobile industry, etc., so it is expected that there will be panic in the market. However, the market is trending higher, and prices are rising slightly, at most by 2 pounds. Automobile and steel stocks are being bought. It is generally believed that the revised exchange management plan is not as objectionable as the original plan, but it is still hoped that there will be further amendments. Mussolini's Bombastic Remarks Disrupt European Situation 58

Africa is Italy's Fourth Coast; Franco-Italian Dispute Takes a Further Step

(London) Mussolini's speech at the Second Five-Year Congress of the Fascist Party not only caused deep reflection in Europe but was also unanimously regarded in London as a clear sign of more troubles to come. The Franco-Italian conflict began with the status of Italians in Tunis and the difficulty in easing the situation. Italy has recently made strides in Africa through its military and economic organizations, and it has even intensified domestic propaganda by appropriating the statement that Africa is Italy's fourth coast. In the past eight years, Italy's influence in Africa has grown surprisingly. There are many books on this matter, and Mussolini has even written prefaces for them. The appointment of Italy's most famous aviator, General Balbo, as the Governor of Libya a few months ago is another indication of Italy's emphasis on Africa. This speech, delivered after the establishment of the Danube Pact, which made Italy appear to be the protector of Austria and Hungary, is said to contain even deeper meaning. Carefully examining Mussolini's remarks regarding Germany, disarmament, and the future of the League of Nations, and his tone in identifying Fascism as a political system that would make Rome admired by all, reminds one of previous predictions that Mussolini's ambition is to make Italy the leader of the world. This makes one feel that there is increasing evidence to support this. (Special Telegram from the Japan Times, 19th)

Italy, Austria, and Hungary Reach Agreement 59

Germany Expresses Non-Participation, Believing it Will Create Future Disputes

(Berlin) Since the publication of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's remarks on Sunday, the semi-official foreign affairs commentary newspaper here has published an article expressing considerable satisfaction with Mussolini's remarks, saying that all kinds of speculation in the outside world about Italy's attitude can be cleared up, and it is particularly pragmatic to maintain Germany's important sovereignty and does not contradict its original purpose. As for the Three-Nation Agreement, although it is not necessary to exaggerate its importance too much, the method it adopts is quite similar to the methods France is accustomed to using. Therefore, this kind of solidarity is easy to turn into "a tyrannical alliance of countries," which creates future disputes. For this reason, Germany has never been willing to participate in this kind of connection. The agreement states that if one country wishes to consult with each other when any event occurs, they must consult with each other, but the location of the meeting and which country's words are the most powerful among the three countries are also questions. However, the Austrian people are 100% German, and Hungary insists on its independent attitude, so in the future, there may not be a tendency that is incompatible with the interests of the two small countries. From an economic point of view, the achievements of the agreement are not great, because Italy's original proposal was to organize a customs union of Italy, Austria, and Hungary. The newspaper also said that Germany will continue to improve the economic organization of the Danube countries as it has done in the past decade and will protect its own economic interests so that they are not interfered with by one-sided attempts with political purposes. (National Telegram, 19th)

Issues of Sanctions and Security 60

British and French Continue Negotiations; Britain Asks France to Explain Various Wishes

(London) Since the French government sent a reply to the British disarmament memorandum of January 29, the British government has asked the French cabinet to clearly explain France's various wishes regarding sanctions and security guarantees. The British and French will continue to address this issue through diplomatic channels. (Havas, 20th)

France Breaks Up Another German-Russian Espionage Organization 61

Stealing Secret Information from Britain, France, and the United States

(Paris) Today, the French Secret Service discovered a large-scale espionage organization dedicated to stealing secret information from countries such as Britain, France, and the United States for Germany and Soviet Russia. As a result of today's search, a total of sixteen people were arrested, including a professor, and a large number of important documents, codebooks, and maps were seized. This search was based on information provided by the Stevel-Stevelsville couple, who were arrested last December. According to reports, the Stevelsville couple did not reveal the truth until yesterday. Professor Lesch, who was also experimenting at the Paris Biological Institute, is also among the sixteen people. Therefore, the news of Lesch's involvement in the conspiracy has shocked political and scientific circles. The organization is dedicated to investigating the secrets of Britain, the United States, and France on a very large scale, employing a large number of personnel, especially paying attention to news on the army, navy, poison gas, and armaments, as well as commercial data. In addition, a female dentist named Duvisi is also a member of the organization, specializing in delivering secret documents and photographs to various cities in Switzerland, and then transferring them to Moscow and Berlin from there. Professor Lesch receives a monthly salary of 3,000 francs. Most of the other documents concern wartime industrial mobilization plans, and there is also a map registering important factories throughout France. (National Telegram, 20th)

The Situation of Labor-Management Disputes in the United States is Becoming Increasingly Serious 62

Strikes Brewing, Threatening to Affect the Entire Country; Emergency Meeting Held in New York

(Washington) Labor-management conflicts in the United States are erupting from time to time, and the scope of these conflicts threatens to affect the entire country. The three major industries of the nation are particularly hard hit. Therefore, President Roosevelt and Attorney General Cummings convened a meeting here today to discuss opinions on the serious situation, as a general strike would be detrimental to the government's recovery plan. At the same time, industrial leaders gathered in New York to discuss the current situation of the railway and automobile industries. In San Francisco, mediators believe that the dockworkers' strike will indefinitely block the shipping industry on the western coast of the United States. The meeting between the President and the Attorney General at the White House lasted for several hours. After the meeting, rumors spread that the government would take decisive measures when necessary to avert the crisis of a strike. Currently, with the exception of the Ford Motor Company, other prominent American automobile companies have sent representatives to participate in the meeting held in New York. The goal of this meeting is to plan how to deal with future strikes, as strikers have issued threats to disrupt the national automobile industry, causing 250,000 people to stop working, and will directly incite workers in the railway, steel, and coal mining industries. While the industrialists were meeting, the National Automobile Workers Union declared that it had no intention of recognizing the American Federation of Labor and did not want to enter into any contracts with the American Federation of Labor for the sake of the automobile workers. Railway authorities in New York have met with leaders of the American Federation of Labor, but there has been no progress in the wage dispute. Railway strikers claim that if the capitalists do not make concessions, they will bring national transportation to a standstill. Railway representatives insist that railway employees must acknowledge the current wage calculation system and continue it for the next six months. A spokesperson for the union not only rejected this proposal, but also demanded compensation for the one-tenth wage reduction of the previous six months. (National Telegram, 19th)

Detroit: If the labor-management dispute in the American automobile industry is not resolved within two days, it may lead to an unprecedented labor movement in American history. Therefore, automobile industry employers are making another effort today to respond to the workers' demands. The workers are currently opposed to the employers' insistence on forcing workers to join company unions. The National Automobile Industry Association issued an article to the workers today, stating that workers should decide for themselves whether they want to transfer their right to negotiate with the company to labor leaders who make this their profession. The article also asked workers to pay attention to the recent wage increases and reduced working hours in the automobile industry. Representatives of the American Federation of Labor replied that if workers vote in favor of joining the company union after an election is held outside the automobile factory under the supervision of the National Recovery Administration, then the American Federation of Labor will naturally concede. (Reuters Telegram, 19th)

(Washington) Managers of various railway bureaus in the United States met here today and decided on a 15% wage reduction plan, to be implemented from July 1st. Railway employees strongly opposed this, saying that their wages have already been reduced by one-tenth and they are already suffering a great deal. If the reduction is increased to 15%, they will feel even more hardship. Railway employee leaders are now requesting that the wage reduction remain at one-tenth. Railway bureau managers seem willing to discuss the proposal not to implement the new wage reduction plan, which is a positive sign. According to news this evening, discussions on this point are still open. At the same time, the automobile industry also held a closed-door meeting in New York today to discuss the threatened strike of 100,000 workers. Ford did not attend, but General Johnson, director of the National Recovery Administration, participated in the meeting, which shows that the Washington authorities attach great importance to the matter. (Reuters Telegram, 19th)

(New York) The conflict between large industrialists and labor is intensifying, which is an indirect result of the policies implemented by the Economic Recovery Administration. The Economic Recovery Act instructs employers to allow workers to organize unions so that workers can negotiate with employers as a group to resolve disputes when there are conflicts. The current chaos and brewing strikes arise from this. The wave of strikes is spreading to industrial areas, and the most important industries are being threatened. The scope of the conflict was originally limited to automobile industry employers and the American Federation of Labor, but now railway, steel, and California dockworkers have also entered the vortex. In Cranford City, thousands of factory workers have gone on strike. In Tacoma, Washington, 6,616 dockworkers have decided to strike. On the Pacific coast, 60,800 dockworkers have decided that if employers do not recognize the union and allow for reduced working hours and increased wages, they will also take the same action. Chaos and strikes have also occurred in Harrisburg, Pennsylvania, and Indianapolis, Indiana. At the same time, employers are also holding meetings to discuss the situation. They have petitioned Congress to request that Senator Wagner of New York's bill to establish a national permanent labor affairs bureau be rejected. The reason is that if this labor affairs bureau is established, industry and commerce will be controlled by small groups composed of union leaders. In addition, more than 50 large industrial companies in Pennsylvania, Ohio, Maryland, and West Virginia also demanded its cancellation, arguing that Wagner's proposal would lead to the danger of worker autocracy. The labor-management conflict has reached a deadlock, and the situation is roughly as follows: employers declare that they cannot obey the orders arbitrarily issued by the American Federation of Labor. Union leaders say that employers are trying to get workers to join employer-organized unions, so no compromise can be reached. The general public believes that if the American Federation of Labor issues a strike order, the number of workers in the automobile industry and its related industries who will stop working will reach 250,000. This attitude will greatly undermine Roosevelt's economic recovery plan. Roosevelt held a special meeting with Attorney General Cummings this afternoon to study some legal issues because each party has its own interpretation of the industry regulations set by the Recovery Administration. (Havas Telegram, 19th)

Unemployment Situation in Europe 63

(London) According to statistics released today by the British Ministry of Labour, the unemployment situation in Europe last year showed little progress compared to 1932. The number of unemployed in Britain decreased by 220,000, and in Germany it also decreased by 850,000. However, the situation in Italy, the Netherlands, and Austria is worse than before. (Reuters Telegram, 20th)

Waksugi Appointed First Secretary of the Japanese Embassy 64

(Tokyo) Waksugi Yo, the former Consul General in San Francisco who has now returned to the country, was appointed First Secretary of the Japanese Embassy in Peiping on the 20th. He is scheduled to depart from Tokyo on the 25th to take office. The current secretary of the embassy, Nakayama Shoichi, is reportedly to be transferred to Hamburg, Germany, as Consul General. (Japanese Union Telegram, 20th)

(A) Founding members, that is, countries listed in the Covenant. Brazil notified its withdrawal on June 14, 1926, and officially withdrew on June 13, 1928. Japan notified its withdrawal on March 27, 1933.

(B) Invited to join and also listed in the Covenant. These countries deposited a declaration of participation in the Covenant with the Secretariat within two months of the Covenant taking effect.

Argentina has not sent representatives to attend since its delegation withdrew from the First Assembly and notified on September 26, 1933, that its Congress had approved the League of Nations Covenant.

Colombia's participation in the Covenant was conditional on naturally not recognizing the Republic of Panama.

Spain notified its withdrawal on September 8, 1926, but declared on March 20, 1928, that it would remain a member. Switzerland declared that it would assume all the responsibilities of a League of Nations member, and the Administrative Council considered that the country's permanent neutrality and the guarantee of its territorial integrity were not in conflict with the Covenant.

(C) Joined after the Covenant came into effect. Costa Rica joined on December 16, 1920, but notified its withdrawal on December 24, 1924, and officially withdrew on January 1, 1927. Mexico notified its withdrawal on December 14, 1932. Germany notified its withdrawal on October 14, 1933.

Withdrawal Procedure: Any member may withdraw from the League after giving two years' prior notice, but upon withdrawal, it must have fully discharged all its international obligations and all obligations under this Covenant (Article 1, Paragraph 3 of the Covenant). Any member may freely disapprove of an amendment to the Covenant, but from that time it shall cease to be a member of the League (Article 26, Paragraph 2 of the Covenant).

Central Meteorological Observatory Reports on the Earthquake in the Han-Wu Area 67

(Nanjing) The Central Meteorological Observatory reported that at 8:00 AM on the 18th, a slight earthquake was felt in the Han-Wu Anqing area. The observatory's seismograph began recording at 8:18:12 AM, lasting for more than two minutes. The nature was rapid, and the calculated direction was slightly west of south, 270 kilometers (478 li) from Beijing. The epicenter was located between Anqing, Zhenshan, and Qian Mountain, and the depth of the fault could be 30 to 40 kilometers. Since the epicenter was located in a mountainous area and the intensity of the earthquake was weak, it would not cause any disasters or losses. There were also two small earthquakes between 4:54 and 4:57 AM, which may have been precursors to the earthquake, but the intensity was very weak. The earthquake was also felt in Hankou. (Central News Agency Telegram, 20th)

Administrative Conference of Eleven Provinces Opens 68

More than 70 People Arrive, Including Commissioners of Civil Affairs and Education from Various Provinces

Reports on the Progress of Governance, Discussion of Various Recommendations

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang, in order to improve the administration of various provinces and promote the post-banditry schemes in the banditry-affected areas, has specially convened the Secretaries-General, Commissioners of Civil Affairs and Education of the eleven provinces, and the Commissioners of the various provinces where administrative supervisory commissioners have been established, to come to Jiangxi for a meeting, to personally examine and instruct them. Those who have been summoned have arrived in the province one after another in recent days, drafting reports and suggestions, which they have submitted to Chiang for review. The formal meeting was held on the 18th in the conference hall of the Headquarters. Those who attended included: Cheng Tianfang, Secretary-General of the Jiangsu Provincial Government; Zhou Fohai, Commissioner of Education; Gu Renfa, Commissioner of Civil Affairs; Lu Dai, Lu Bisu, Chen Bulei from Zhejiang; Li Zuyu, Zheng Zhenwen from Fujian; Chen Shikai, Ma Lingfu, Yang Lian from Anhui; Meng Guangpeng, Cheng Qibao from Hubei; Fang Qidao, Li Peiji, Qi Zhenru from Henan; Li Jizhong, Shui Zi from Gansu; Geng Shoubo, Peng Yuwei, Zhou Xuechang from Shaanxi; Yi Shuzhu, Cao Dianqiu, Zhu Jingnong from Hunan; Liu Tigan, Zhu Huaibing, Cheng Shijun from Jiangxi; Li Anguo, Administrative Supervisory Commissioner for Bandit Suppression in Sichuan; E Xiang, Lu Xian, Yuan Luoan, Cheng Ruhai, Shi Yuling, Li Jiading, Liu Fu, Yang Enxi, Li Guojun, Yuan Dianshu, Lei Xiaocen from Hubei; Wang Fanqi, Zhu Zhirong, Ouyang Zhen, Fang Dingzhong, Guo Jingdai, Tang Ken from Henan; Wang Hantao, He Haoran, Xu Panwen, Luo Shishi, Huang Renwang from Zhejiang; Xiang Naiqi, Xu Peinan, Xu Yaping from Anhui; Wei Suzhong, Zhang Chi, Hua Guang, Zhou Zuofu, Li Zhengyi, Wang Youlan, Guo Su from Jiangxi; Xiong Shihui, Director of the Headquarters Office; He Guoguang, Commissioner of the First Department; Yang Yongtai, Commissioner of the Second Department; and more than 70 others. At a little after 9 o'clock, Chairman Chiang arrived and the meeting began with music. Chairman Chiang delivered a speech after the usual formalities, first reporting the significance of convening this meeting, hoping that all administrative officials would eradicate all past malpractices and revitalize the administration. After the speech, representatives from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other provinces reported on the administrative, civil, financial, educational, construction, and self-defense situations of their respective provincial governments. The meeting adjourned at 12 o'clock. The second general meeting continued at 2 PM, with commissioners from various provinces and administrative regions reporting on their administrative progress and the progress of post-banditry and self-defense. The morning of the 19th was a memorial week, with a general meeting in the afternoon and a closing ceremony on the morning of the 20th. Chiang will also meet with and examine each of them individually and give instructions on everything. It is reported that a total of sixty or seventy reports and suggestions have been received from various provinces and administrative regions, which have been sorted and classified by the Second Department of the Headquarters and listed as proposals for discussion on a case-by-case basis. (18th)

Red Bandits Suffer a Crushing Defeat in Nanfeng 69

Main Force of Pseudo 1359 and Other Army Corps Badly Defeated

Nanchang Correspondence: Military news, the pseudo First, Third, Fifth, Ninth, Twelfth Army Corps, and the Guard Division, after recent reorganization and replenishment, sneaked from Guangchang on the Grey Day to the Baijinsha and Pingshang areas southwest of Nanfeng, concentrating their forces to attack our Chen positions of the Northern Route Army. At dawn, the pseudo First, Third, and Ninth Army Corps, and the first part of the pseudo Fifth Army Corps, simultaneously advanced towards our positions at Wuduzhai, Donghuashan, Shigushan, Yanglindu, and other places. Another part, via Sanxi Yangmeizhai, made a roundabout attack on our right flank, engaging our Third Route Army in fierce fighting all day long, with the fiercest fighting at Wuduzhai. After fierce attacks by our defending soldiers, they did not succeed. At noon on the Yuan Day, the bandits once again launched a fierce attack on our Yangmeizhai Jianling Chen positions with their main force. Our Third Route Army then launched attacks in several directions. After 4 o'clock, the bandits were surrounded and could not take care of each other from beginning to end, suffering heavy casualties, and retreated in the southwest direction. On the Cold Day, our pursuing troops surrounded and suppressed them in the areas of Zuoqiaotou Ganfang Zhufang. In this bloody battle lasting four days and four nights, the bandits suffered more than 8,000 casualties, with about 3,000 corpses in front of the battle, and more than 20 bandit soldiers were captured alive, and thousands of guns were seized. The detailed number is still being checked. Our side also suffered nearly a thousand casualties. From then on, the bandits' courage has been chilled, and it will not be difficult to annihilate them as scheduled and achieve a complete victory.

Another message, the Headquarters announced that at midnight on the Yu Day, our guerrillas encountered bandits three miles from the Tatai Three Platforms. After an interception by one of our units, the bandits turned north and fled to Guishi Ridge. After two of our units worked together to follow and encircle them, the bandits began to collapse completely and fled to Huaping. In this battle, which lasted about six or seven hours, 700 to 800 bandits were killed, 10 bandits were captured, and 1 machine gun, 3 submachine guns, and more than 200 rifles were seized. In addition, on the 13th, Anfu County sent troops to suppress bandits in Qingshan, seizing 12 bandit guns. The Volunteers of the 81st District sent troops to suppress bandits in Yejikeng, seizing 25 bandit guns. The Yihuang Volunteer Brigade attacked bandits in Huoyuan on the Yuan (13th) evening, killing several members of the pseudo-prosecution team. On the same evening, the Volunteers of the Fourth District sent troops to suppress bandits in Qidu, killing a pseudo-military minister in Makeng, capturing 5 bandits, and seizing 6 rifles, reactionary documents, and a package of pseudo-chops. (Datong News Agency, March 17th)

Bandit Suppression Begins in Eastern Fujian 70

Bandit Gangs Burning and Killing Everywhere, Very Tragic

Wang Jingjiu Has Led Troops to Suppress Them

Fuzhou Correspondence: The reorganization of the militia in Fujian Province has been completed. Regarding bandit suppression matters, great progress has already been made in northern Fujian. In eastern Fujian, it has also been launched, jointly presided over by the Fuzhou Headquarters, the Provincial Government, and the Mawei Naval Port Headquarters. The eastern Fujian region includes 15 counties under the former Mindao Circuit, which were divided into Fuzhou and Funing Prefectures in the former Qing Dynasty. The counties where the Red bandits are rampant are Fuding, Shouning, Xiapu, Ningde, and Fuan under the jurisdiction of Funing Prefecture, and Lianjiang, Luoyuan, Pingnan, and Pingtan under the jurisdiction of Fuzhou Prefecture. However, because the area is bordered by the East Sea on one side and connected to Zhejiang on the other, the bandits' traces are extremely elusive. Therefore, although the naval and land fleets and the Fujian and Zhejiang troops have repeatedly launched large-scale joint suppressions, it has been difficult to eliminate them. Recently, the authorities have repeatedly received reports from various county governments and social groups about the critical situation. The cities of Luoyuan, Xiapu, and Shouning Counties have all been surrounded, and the cities and towns of Lianjiang, Luoding, and Ningde have all been looted. It has been found that the bandits in these nine counties are purely local communists, gathered from hooligans and local ruffians. They are called guerrillas or Red Guards, with each gang ranging from a hundred to several hundred people. Every time they capture a township, they set up a pseudo-township Soviet government. Every time they capture a district, they set up a pseudo-district committee, appointing local ruffians as chairmen or members, and looting everywhere. Anyone who has a little property or has any grievances is destroyed. According to a recent report from the Lianjiang Bandit Suppression Committee, in the sixth and seventh districts of the county alone, since January of this year, dozens of district chiefs, township chiefs, Jia chiefs, grain communists, and gentry have been killed, hundreds of men, women, old, and young have been burned to death, more than a hundred houses have been burned down, and more than 100,000 yuan has been looted from shops. All the deeds and certificates owned by the people have been burned to ashes. Lianjiang is a county close to the province, and it is still so rampant. It is conceivable how tragic the coastal areas and the villages in the mountains have suffered. The authorities also believe that it cannot be ignored, so they specially dispatched Wang Jingjiu, the commander of the 87th Division stationed in Fuzhou, to lead troops to suppress them on a large scale the day before yesterday. Wang has now arrived in Ningde, and as soon as he summons the county magistrates of each county to talk and inquire about the bandit situation, he can start the suppression. However, the Weiduo regiment of the Marine Corps stationed in Lianjiang has already breached the bandit dens in Toubao, Ma, Danyang, and Xiaoao in the sixth and seventh districts and is currently carrying out the Qingxiang campaign. (March 17th)

川匪 Abandon Nanba 71

Chuan Army Advances on Three Sides, Gains Advantage Repeatedly

Xu Bandit Leads Remnants to Retreat North to Tongjiang

Hankou Correspondence: After the Guominjun recovered various counties, including Qu, Ying, Peng, Yi, Sui, and Xuan, from Xu Xiangqian's remaining bandit forces in Sichuan, the occupied area has decreased daily, and their power has gradually waned. Consequently, they shortened the battle lines, fortifying the three counties of Tongjiang, Nanjiang, and Bazhong. Liu Xiang, the Commander-in-Chief of the Sichuan Bandit Suppression, having completed the first phase of the suppression plan, convened the second phase suppression conference in Chengdu. After determining the strategies, he ordered a general offensive, designating Bazhong as the target. In recent days, the 3rd and 5th Route Armies have joined forces there. The 3rd Route Army, led by Li Qixiang and Luo Zezhou, captured Shuangmiao Chang and Xingling Chang on the 13th. The following day, Luo's troops also captured Enyang River, 60 li from Ba. On the same day, the 5th Route Army, led by Fan Shaozeng, launched a fierce assault with suicide squads towards the Honglingtai mountain range, advancing to the line of Honglingtai, Guanzi Zhai, and Yinyang Mountain. The Enyang River is a crucial pass for Bazhong, and fierce hand-to-hand combat ensued, resulting in many casualties. Honglingtai is a well-known natural stronghold, and the battle was especially fierce. The bandits were unable to hold and collapsed in retreat. Currently, the 2nd Route Army, led by Tian Songyao, has also been ordered to join in. Within days, they will encircle Ba city on three sides. The 1st Route Army, led by Deng Xihou, will launch a flanking attack from Wangcang towards Mumen, solely responsible for the northern front, remotely supporting the attack on Ba. On the bandit side, there are five pseudo-armies: the 4th, 9th, 25th, 30th, and 31st. The pseudo-4th Army suffered 80-90% losses in strength during the various battles in Suiyi over a month. It is confirmed that the pseudo-army commander, He Wei, has been killed in action. Xu bandit, facing the critical situation in Ba city, launched a counter-attack but failed. He has plans to abandon Ba and Nan. Therefore, only the pseudo-9th Army, pseudo-30th Army, and guerrillas defend Ba and Nan, while the main force has moved to Tongjiang. Ba and Nan depend on each other like lips and teeth. If Bazhong is lost, it will be difficult to defend Nanjiang for long. According to captured bandits, after being defeated by the Central Army in the Henan-Hubei border region in 1932, they held a military conference. Xu Xiangqian advocated fleeing to Gansu and Xinjiang to open up an international route, while Kuang Jixun advocated fleeing to Sichuan. After fighting with Yang and Tian, they were very successful, so they decided to go deep into Sichuan and planned to seize Kuiwan and connect with He bandit, using Sichuan and Hubei as their base. After entering Sichuan, more than half of the original soldiers were killed or wounded. The newly formed troops are mostly Sichuanese, who are not good at fighting. Subsequently, they suffered repeated defeats. Xu bandit blamed Kuang bandit and killed him. Now, Xu bandit and key bandits such as Chen Changhao have decided to move their headquarters to Tongjiang, considering the critical situation in Bazhong. The ammunition factory, mint, grain depot, and communication organs are all located there. Therefore, it is credible that the bandits will abandon Nanba and retreat to Tongjiang. It is not without a plan. It is said that they will first use the main force to defend Tongjiang. If the Guominjun advances too far, they will enter Shaanxi from Chengkou and flee to northern Hubei, and then wander around the border between Shaanxi, Hubei, and Henan, observing the situation and avoiding strength while attacking weakness. The border area between Sichuan, Shaanxi, Hubei, and Henan is mostly high mountains and deep valleys, stretching for thousands of miles, and has not been developed. If the bandits flee there, it will be like a tiger entering the mountains, even more uncontrollable. It is heard that He Chengjun has been ordered to go to Xiangfan, in order to prepare for the prevention of the Sichuan bandits from fleeing into the Hubei-Henan border. (17th)

Lu Province Strictly Guards Against Liu Bandit's Return 72

Sun Tongxuan Appointed Commander of Lunan Garrison

Cavalry Regiment Deployed to Defend Caozhou Area

Jinan Correspondence: Last year, Liu Guitang's remnant bandits fled south, ravaging the border areas of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, as well as the Pinghan Railway line, causing great suffering to the people. Recently, after being pursued by the Henan army, they fled east again, showing a strong tendency to re-enter their old nest in southern Shandong. Liu Zhi, the chairman of Henan, has telegraphed Han Fuju, the chairman of Shandong Province, to prepare for joint suppression. Han has decided to jointly block and intercept them to prevent future troubles. He has appointed Sun Tongxuan, the commander of the 20th Division, as the commander of the Lunan Garrison, and Gu Liangyou, the commander of the Luxi Militia, as the deputy commander, to strengthen vigilance and implement blocking measures. The cavalry regiment led by Li Xuande, stationed in Yucheng, northern Shandong, has been transferred to Jining and Caozhou in southwestern Shandong for guard duty. It is reported that the 1st and 4th companies of the cavalry regiment and the machine gun company, along with the regimental headquarters, were personally led by Li Xuande at 3:00 am today (17th) and took a Jinpu special train to Yanzhou via Jinan. The 2nd and 3rd companies and the transportation platoon, led by Staff Officer Zhao Yiquan, will also pass through Jinan at 2:00 pm today to deploy for defense and jointly block Liu bandit's return. Sun Tongxuan, the commander of the 20th Division, has been ordered to concurrently serve as the commander of the Lunan Garrison and will take the Pinghu train No. 301 to Yanzhou at 9:00 pm tonight to be responsible for the suppression. According to Sun, "I am ordered by Chairman Han to prevent Liu Guitang's remnant bandits from fleeing into Shandong, so I am returning to Yanzhou to arrange everything. As for the actual strength of Liu bandits, it has been greatly reduced, with only one to two thousand people. It is heard that they have fled to Guide in eastern Henan and are still fleeing, showing a strong tendency to flee back to their old nest. As for the defense measures in this province, it needs to be decided after arriving in Yanzhou. The cavalry regiment led by Regiment Commander Li has also been ordered to go south and passed through Jinan this morning, first arriving in Yanzhou. Its defense location is planned in the Caozhou area. As for the remaining forces of Liu bandits, it will definitely not be a problem in the future." (17th)

Zhu Jiajua Speaks on New Life Movement and Education 74

Beijing News: The Central Party Headquarters held the 122nd weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen at 9:00 am today (19th). Central Committee members Ye Chucang, Zhu Jiajua, Xiao Jishan, Hong Ludong, Wang Luyi, Chen Qianjun, Li Zonghuang, Ke Xing'e, Bai Yunti, and central comrades attended, totaling more than 500 people. Chairman Ye Chucang presided over the ceremony. Committee Member Zhu Jiajua then gave a report titled "New Life Movement and Education." The original text is as follows:

"When the Capital New Life Movement Promotion Association was established, Jiajua explained the meaning of the movement in detail. The New Life Movement is a great movement for national revival. It arises from the urgent demands of the nation to perform the spirit of the times. Its foundation is propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame. It is initiated by the spirit of national history and also takes the mission of promoting the spirit of national history. We must start from daily life and extend to the entire life. We must start from personal life and extend to national life. We must practice what we preach and seek to influence with sincerity, purely cultivate ourselves to create an atmosphere, so as to revive our nation and build our country. In addition to implementing and promoting our movement according to these principles, we also pay attention to the new life of future figures in society. Therefore, the issue of education is closely related to this movement. Jiajua relies on past experience, and has not left the education sector in the past 20 years, so I would like to say a few words here.

Mr. Chiang Kai-shek witnessed the difficulties of the times, so he launched this movement. He knows the shortcomings of our nation now, so he especially pays attention to the cultivation of the four inherent virtues of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame. Starting from personal daily life, observing propriety starts from cleanliness, understanding righteousness starts from keeping promises, cultivating integrity starts from frugality and simplicity, and knowing shame starts from being responsible. However, is the general life of the Chinese people like this now? Romantic decadence, disunity and superficiality, lack of courtesy, no discipline, no order, no sense of responsibility, as well as corruption and various evils. I think one of the biggest reasons is that education in the past had no purpose, no policy, and no methods. The spirit of the modern Chinese nation has gradually declined. By the end of the Qing Dynasty, it was oppressed by various countries and struggled several times. Seeing the Boxer Movement as the final failure, the nation's self-confidence was completely lost. Since then, all reform movements have imitated foreign countries in everything, blindly following suit. As a result, the inherent historical spirit of China was completely lost. Foreign policies and systems, regardless of whether they are in line with national conditions, are mostly taken as good prescriptions for curing China. All kinds of cosmopolitanism, anarchism, communism, liberalism, etc., have resulted in the complete collapse of China's systems and cultural relics, creating a chaotic situation. Therefore, the young people created during this period are scattered to the society and sow many roots of disaster, damaging the country's vitality. Isn't this the fault of past education?

Therefore, when our party set its capital in Nanjing and began state construction, it first urged the determination of educational goals based on Premier Sun Yat-sen's teachings, standing on its own historical spirit to revive the spirit of our nation. At that time, Sun Yat-sen University, together with the education departments of Guangdong and Guangxi, proposed the case of establishing the Three Principles of the People's national education to save the country from danger at the 17th National Education Conference, which was finally revised and passed. The purpose of education was gradually determined to be the revival of the nation. The Second Plenary Session of the Fourth Central Committee, the Fifth Plenary Session of the Second Central Committee, the Third National Congress, the Fourth National Congress, and the National Conference of our party, regarding educational resolutions, and the provisions of the Constitution and the National Education Chapter, have constantly taken national revival as the consistent purpose of education. After the September 18th Incident, we further sought policies and methods to implement this determined purpose. During this period, the government first issued strict orders to reorganize universities, reducing and merging university departments, improving university content, rectifying academic style, paying attention to practical subjects, establishing scientific terms, and implementing the ban on universities with incomplete equipment and corrupt content. Then, the organization of primary schools to universities was reorganized as a whole. On the one hand, in addition to the original school system, short-term compulsory education methods were implemented to make compulsory education easier to popularize and rapidly promote. The two-part system of primary schools was advocated to save expenses and increase opportunities for children to enter school. The curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools were determined, and a complete set of textbooks for primary and secondary schools, as well as Mongolian, Hui, and Tibetan textbooks, were compiled one after another, so that the teaching materials contain historical spirit and focus on national revival to inspire students to love the country and the nation and respect their own historical spirit. More stringent regulations were made on the service of teachers to cultivate discipline. These policies and methods implemented according to the educational goals of our party were expanded in their implementation by the various resolutions of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Second Central Committee of our party to reorganize national education. These organizational policies and methods of the Ministry of Education in the past two or three years are constantly being carried out. Although there are many obstacles, the results are not easy to see quickly. However, these obstacles are naturally because most people in society do not understand the spirit of national history, so it is not easy to promote educational policies and systems built according to the spirit of national history. Therefore, the New Life Movement is also deeply related to education.

Mr. Chiang Kai-shek launched the New Life Movement this time to transform the entire society and reform all undertakings, and also to use the entire strength of the society to promote the improvement of education, so as to save the nation from danger. Therefore, we should promote the New Life Movement in accordance with this purpose. At the same time, we must know that the New Life Movement must work hard on education and must cultivate the habits of the new life when pure young people are not deeply infected.

In the past few years, we have sown many seeds of national revival in education. The germination, development, and growth of these many seeds depend entirely on the promotion of the strength of the entire society, that is to say, the power of social promotion will definitely be after the success of the new life. There is no doubt that the New Life Movement is particularly deeply related to education, so it is necessary to put forward an explanation."

All Buddhist Statues on Tianlong Mountain Stolen and Sold by Traitors 75

Statistics Show the Number of Buddhist Statues, Large and Small, to be About One Hundred

Traitors Stole Them in an Organized Manner

The Main Culprit Arrested in Ping and Sent to Jin for Trial

Beijing News: Among the Buddhist grottoes in our country, the most famous are the Thousand Buddha Caves in Dunhuang, the Yungang Grottoes in Datong, the Longmen Grottoes in Luoyang, and the Tianlong Mountain Grottoes in Taiyuan. The Shenghousi Grottoes on Tianlong Mountain were carved in the Northern Qi Dynasty. Their style and form are unique compared with the Thousand Buddha Caves, Yungang, and Longmen Grottoes carved in the Northern Wei, Sui, and Tang Dynasties. Moreover, there are very few stone carvings of Emperor Taizong of the Northern Qi Dynasty handed down, which is even more precious. The mountain is about 45 li south of the current provincial capital, which is the ancient Jinyang. Emperor Gao Huan, the founder of the Northern Qi Dynasty, once built a palace here to escape the summer heat. His son, Emperor Wenxuan, rebuilt many temples on the mountain. Now they are all damaged, except for Shenghousi, which stands alone. The temple was built in the first year of Huangjian. It is said that there are 24 grottoes inside, with statistics of about one hundred statues, large and small. In recent years, more and more Chinese and foreign scholars have traveled far to visit. Ignorant villagers occasionally shaved off Buddhist statues and sold them to foreigners. However, the damage caused by petty theft was limited. Most of them can still maintain their original appearance for people to study. Unexpectedly, bad news came last year that all the statues in the grottoes of the temple were chiseled out and transported to foreigners in large quantities. Only one stone Buddha about 24 feet high remained in the temple, but its eyes were also destroyed. This must be because it was too high and could not be moved and sold, so they were angry and did this crazy thing. In addition, the statues, regardless of size, only have traces of axes and chisels left. Even the small statues on the top of the cave were chiseled away. The only remaining Buddhist art of the Northern Qi Dynasty, which has survived for 1,400 years, has since bid farewell to our Chinese people and can never be seen again. It is said that the average price per statue is 10,000 yuan. The traitors only got a million silver dollars. After the academic circles in Beiping heard about it, they sent personnel from the Antiquities Preservation Association to conduct an on-site investigation. They were very sad and indignant and repeatedly thought about investigating and detaining them nearby for investigation. However, the other party's method of transportation and sale was extremely cunning and secret, making it difficult to capture them. Until last winter, personnel from the History Museum affiliated to the Academia Sinica discovered a small batch of flying statues being transported from Jin to Ping for sale. They immediately reported to the personnel of the Antiquities Preservation Association to disguise and investigate. After obtaining conclusive evidence, they notified the Beiping Municipal Public Security Bureau to send police to a certain hotel in Changxiang Er Tiao to arrest the shopkeeper surnamed Zhang. According to his confession, the stone statues were mortgaged to a certain Chinese by industry insiders, and he also confessed that they were deposited by Hou, the owner of a hotel in Taiyuan. The Beiping Municipal Public Security Bureau ordered the arrest of Hou, who has now been arrested and is being tried by the Taiyuan Court. According to rumors, the chiseling of the stone statues was a large-scale and organized operation. Many people armed with weapons surrounded the temple on the mountain for several days, working leisurely inside and transporting them away in batches. This statement remains to be verified. However, since the case is so serious, it cannot be handled by one or two merchants. It can be asserted that we will see how the court handles the case to find out the truth.

Hai Jun Asks to Expedite Construction of Xisha Island Observatory 76

Construction Proposal Already Approved by the Government

The Ministry of Finance Has Repeatedly Delayed Due to Lack of Funds

We Still Neglect It, Fearing It Will Be Occupied by the French

Beijing News: The Ministry of Navy reported that the construction of an observatory on Dongsha Island, Hainan, will report the climate, facilitate shipping, and benefit both China and foreign countries. The observatory on Xisha Island is also being planned and constructed, but it has not yet started due to lack of funds. However, the island is not far from French Annam, and the French have long thought of getting involved. Recently, newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai published reports that French newspapers are advocating the occupation of Xisha. The Ministry of Navy, seeing the critical situation, again submitted a request to the Executive Yuan yesterday, asking it to pay attention, stating, "The territory of Xisha is related to national sovereignty and diplomacy. In the summer of the 14th year of the Republic of China (1925), the former Ministry of Navy proposed a cabinet meeting and decided to establish an observatory on the island. After the establishment of this ministry, it again jointly submitted a request to your Yuan (Executive Yuan) with the Ministry of Communications on July 4, 1930, to forward it to the National Government, ordering the Ministry of Finance to quickly allocate the estimated 180,000 yuan needed to build the island's radio observatory and other expenses on schedule. Later, it was instructed by your Yuan in July of the same year that 'This case has been submitted to the 77th meeting of this Yuan, and it was resolved to follow the report of the two ministries, which has been forwarded to the National Government and ordered the Ministry of Finance and the Guangdong Provincial Government to comply.' The Ministry of Navy compiled a budget and contacted the Ministry of Finance to receive the funds. However, the construction was delayed due to the Ministry of Finance not allocating funds. In March 1932, the Ministry of Navy approved the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' consultation, stating that the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs claimed that the kings of Annam Jia Long had erected monuments and built towers on the island a hundred years ago, and asserted Annam's prior rights, and asked our country to explain according to law. Seeing that the establishment of a station on Dongsha had solved the territorial issue, Xisha still needs to establish a station, and the French are citing unfounded claims, intending to occupy it, it again submitted a request to your Yuan on April 1, 1932, stating that the establishment of a station on the island is of great importance, and if it is not done now, the consequences will be difficult to imagine. It is still requested to order the Ministry of Finance to investigate the case and allocate funds. Subsequently, it was instructed by your Yuan in April that 'This case has been submitted to a meeting of this Yuan and resolved to order the Ministry of Finance to allocate the funds in installments within six months to finance the project.' In addition to ordering the Ministry of Finance to comply, please be informed. The ministry then consulted the Ministry of Finance for allocation of funds and planned to proceed with everything. Later, the Ministry of Finance replied that it was financially exhausted and had no funds to allocate. The Ministry again submitted a request to your Yuan in mid-May, and it was instructed that 'This case was recently submitted by the Ministry of Finance, stating that it was financially exhausted and had no funds to allocate, and it was instructed to make efforts to raise funds.' Later, it was instructed by your Yuan in May that 'According to the Ministry of Finance's report, the Executive Yuan telegraphed to order that the case of the Navy requesting the allocation of 180,000 yuan to build the Xisha Island radio observatory should still follow the previous order to make efforts to raise funds. It was previously ordered by the Executive Yuan that, in the period of national crisis, financial stagnation, and extreme financial exhaustion, maintaining the status quo was already difficult. The previous expenses were so large that it was really impossible to allocate funds at one time, and the situation has been reported. Now, with the previous cause, although the current situation has slightly eased, the source of finance is still exhausted. It is only hoped that the previous expenses can be given more time, and once the finances are slightly better, they will be allocated in accordance with the instructions.' Therefore, the establishment of a station on the island has been suspended to this day and has not been started. On the 7th of this month, newspapers in Shanghai and Beijing published that French newspapers recently advocated occupying the Xisha Islands, the biggest reason being that the Xisha Islands are the inevitable route for hurricanes to invade Annam in summer and autumn. The island has no meteorological station, and the Annam area cannot receive meteorological reports in advance, so it is difficult to prepare, so it is difficult to implement unless it is occupied in time. The Ministry of Navy has repeatedly stated the importance of the island and the urgent need to establish a station in its reports in July 1930 and April 1932. Now that the French newspapers have such remarks, if we do not act again, it is hard to guarantee that it will not become a reality. Weighing the urgency of the matter, it is really impossible to delay the construction of the station. What should be done to prevent coveting and protect national sovereignty? We hereby submit a document for your review and implementation."

A Traveler at the Huashang Hotel in Huashang Commits Suicide by Poisoning 78

On the 16th of this month, a traveler who claimed to be Wu Shan, 26 years old, came to Huashang Hotel on Tongyun Road in this city from Su and booked room No. 2. On the 17th, he left. On the 18th, the traveler hurriedly came to Huashang Hotel again and stayed in room No. 2 under the name of Wu Shan. On the same day, he visited Meiyuan and other famous attractions and returned to the hotel without any abnormality. Yesterday (20th) at 11:00 am, the teahouse waiter Xu Jingxian called Wu Shan since he had not gotten up yet, but there was no response. Knowing something was wrong, he went to the balcony from the neighboring room, broke the window and entered the room. He saw that the traveler had already died. He immediately reported to the accountant and forwarded the report to the county court, requesting an autopsy. After receiving the report, the prosecutor's office sent prosecutor Shen, accompanied by coroner Wang, to conduct an autopsy at 4:30 pm. The autopsy revealed that the traveler Wu Shan had blood flowing from his mouth, and his face was slightly blue. It was confirmed that he died of poisoning before his death. After the autopsy, the hotel was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial. The cause of the suicide is nothing more than economic difficulties and broken love.

Provincial Order for All Counties to Establish Female Police Officers 79

The Jiangsu Provincial Government believes that in this era of open social interaction and increasingly complex social situations, relying solely on male police officers is difficult to cover all aspects. Moreover, Jiangsu Province is close to the capital, and all facilities should be a model for other provinces. Female police officers should be established in a timely manner to meet the needs of the environment and ensure social security. Therefore, it specially ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to issue a circular to all counties, ordering them to comply quickly. The original text of the circular is as follows: It is ordered to comply with the fact that in this era of open social interaction between men and women and increasingly complex situations, relying solely on male police officers is difficult to cover all aspects. Female police officers should be established in a timely manner to maintain social stability and prevent future hidden dangers. It is hereby ordered to the authorities of all counties and police agencies to comply with the order and organize quickly, and to report the progress of the work at any time for verification. The measures for establishing female police officers are: 1. The provincial police school should recruit one-tenth of female students in each enrollment to receive the same level of police education as male students. 2. The provincial police training school should recruit one-tenth of female students in each enrollment to receive the same level of primary police education as male police officers. 3. In addition to complying with the regulations of the police academy and police training school, the qualifications for recruiting female police officers are: 1. They must be over 18 years old and under 25 years old. 2. They must be over 4 feet 5 inches tall. 3. They must not have been sentenced to more than one year of imprisonment. 4. Except for detective studies, the courses taught should be taught according to the textbooks of each level of police. 5. After graduating from female police, in addition to special matters that should be paid attention to and efforts made (such as investigating important cases), their tasks are to investigate household registration, inspect, rescue, women and children, and maintain social customs. 6. Except when performing special tasks, female police officers should wear plain clothes. The uniforms they wear should be the same as male police officers, but they should wear black skirts to distinguish them and avoid public misunderstandings.

Yangzhou

Large Number of Opium Offenders Arrested in the City 80

Our county's urban and rural areas are vast and densely populated, making opium suppression and inspection inherently difficult. Furthermore, public security personnel are often suspected of neglecting their duties, and police officers are suspected of extorting money, making it difficult to eradicate opium use. Since County Magistrate Ma took office over a year ago, despite repeated orders for strict prohibition, enforcement has been weak, and the root of the problem has not been eradicated. County Magistrate Ma deeply regretted this, and after a long investigation lasting four months, he secretly verified that there were more than five hundred households operating opium dens. Magistrate Ma remained calm and, on the evening of the 18th, summoned the county detective team and all political police to the county office, ordering them not to leave to prevent leaks. He also secretly summoned the constables from various districts and towns to the county. At approximately 8 p.m. that evening, accompanied by Section Chiefs Yin and Tang, Deputy Chief Commander Lu of the Security Corps, Deputy Captain Zhao of the Police Squad, and others, he led the entire detective team and political police to conduct searches in different areas according to the addresses and registers. The search concluded at dawn the next day. As a result, a total of 125 male and female offenders were arrested, and hundreds of sets of opium paraphernalia were seized. They were subsequently escorted to the county government for interrogation and required to sign pledges for further investigation.

Taicang

Major Fire in Liuhe Town 81

In Liuhe Town, Second District, a fire broke out at the residence of a Mr. Li in Xiaozhadao, Jiancheng Street, at around 1 p.m. on the 18th due to carelessness while boiling water for laundry, igniting straw. The fire quickly spread through the roof and could not be extinguished, consuming more than sixty homes and destroying over three hundred houses. Two elderly women perished in the blaze. The loss is estimated at tens of thousands of yuan. Liu Xiangqing, an employee of the Liuhe Bus Station, fell into the fire while attempting to extinguish it from the roof, sustaining severe injuries. He was immediately taken to Huizhong Hospital for treatment. His condition is reportedly critical, and his life is in danger.

Local News

Lang Guanpu Discusses Sino-Japanese War Preparations 83

Ma Zhanshan's Plans to go Abroad have been Abandoned

Lang Guanpu, the former acting chairman of Heilongjiang Province, recently arrived in Shanghai from Beiping. A Datong News Agency reporter interviewed Mr. Lang at his residence. Given Mr. Lang's long-term presence in the Northeast, his understanding of Sino-Japanese relations is particularly clear. The reporter inquired about the recent Sino-Japanese situation in detail. He said that since Japan seized our Northeast, the Sino-Japanese situation has obviously shifted from

side conflicts to direct conflict. Japan's recent return of the various passes of the Great Wall to our country is primarily due to its preparation for war against Russia. Most of the so-called Japanese Imperial Army that invaded North China has been transferred to northern Manchuria. Currently, the Japanese authorities believe that Soviet Russia will inevitably become Japan's great enemy in the future. A Sino-Russian war is, in essence, unavoidable. Currently, Japan's national strength is sufficient to defeat Soviet Russia. However, since the success of the first Soviet Five-Year Plan, its national strength has increased significantly. Once its second Five-Year Plan is successful, Japan's national strength will lag behind Soviet Russia. Therefore, the Japanese side

advocates a quick war to occupy the Soviet Russian Maritime Province and Vladivostok, a key port serving as the base for the Soviet Russian navy and air force. Because, geographically, the puppet state of Manchuria is already trapped in a large encirclement of over eight thousand li by Soviet Russia. If Japan waits for the success of the second Soviet Five-Year Plan, Japan risks being defeated by Soviet Russia. The Soviet authorities, due to their unstable position, advocate a slow war to strengthen their national strength. The recent

sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway clearly demonstrates its desire to avoid a conflict with Japan at present. They are vigorously constructing defense works along the border, and the situation is very tense. Therefore, Japan cannot wait for the success of the second Five-Year Plan and will launch a preemptive strike to attack Soviet Russia. The Datong News Agency reporter then inquired about

Mr. Ma Zhanshan's recent situation. Mr. Lang replied that General Ma resides at No. 37, 46th Road, British Concession, Tianjin, rising at 7 a.m. and going to bed at 10 p.m. In his free time, he often chats with former subordinates and reads and practices calligraphy for leisure. Since arriving in Tianjin, he has remained in seclusion. Because a certain country offered a huge sum of 300,000 yuan to purchase a traitor to harm Mr. Ma, Mr. Ma's safety is extremely threatened and he may

relocate to Shanghai. His former subordinates have gradually been reorganized, with only over two thousand remaining under Tan Zixin, currently stationed in Henan under the command of Liu Zhi. There are still over five thousand former subordinates scattered in the Jilin Province, Songhua River, and Hulin areas near the Sino-Russian border. As for General Ma's attitude, he absolutely does not participate in any domestic activities. The issue of going abroad has also been suspended due to the assassination attempt.

Tan Zhen Scheduled to Leave for Overseas Study 84

May 5th

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, Tan Zhen, Vice President of the Judicial Yuan, who was appointed to go to Europe and the United States to study their judiciaries, came to Shanghai to prepare everything. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency spoke with Mr. Tan. According to Mr. Tan, the study tour is now scheduled to depart from Shanghai on the French postal ship *D'Artagnan* on May 5th. He will be accompanied by only three people: Yang Bosen, his English secretary; Li Jing'an, his French secretary; and Jian Bozan, his German secretary. The departure point is France, as the ship is sailing to Marseille. From there, he will proceed to Britain and Germany. He also plans to visit the Soviet Union. The round trip is scheduled for one year. If time permits, he also intends to visit South American countries such as Chile, but this is not certain and will depend on the actual circumstances. Mr. Tan also stated that there are continental and European-American schools of thought in judiciary, and he intends to study both during this trip. However, he will focus primarily on observing the judicial situations in Turkey and Siam. Like our country, Siam and Turkey were once known as the "sick men of East Asia" and have both lost extraterritorial rights. However, Turkey and Siam have both abolished consular jurisdiction and become purely independent nations. However, our country's extraterritorial rights have not yet been recovered. Therefore, this trip will pay particular attention to the judicial conditions in these two countries in order to investigate why our country has not been able to abolish the consular jurisdiction of various countries, whether it is due to the incompetence of our government or whether there are other reasons. Before going abroad, he intends to return to his native Hunan Province, though this intention has not yet been decided. Therefore, whether Mr. Tan's trip to Hunan will materialize remains unknown.

Sichuan Native Place Association Urges Sichuan Shipping Companies 89

To Properly Revise Freight Rates with Various Merchant Groups

To Chongqing Minsheng Company, and to the Sichuan River Allied Shipping Company: We have repeatedly received letters and telegrams from the Chongqing Hardware Association, the Sundries Industry Association, the Piece Goods Merchants, and other merchant groups, all stating that the Sichuan River Alliance has drastically increased freight rates, by as much as two or three times, with the lowest increase being 100 percent. Furthermore, the old custom of deducting the weight of packing materials has been completely abolished, resulting in a sharp increase in freight costs, exceeding the cost of goods by many times. Upon investigation, the Sichuan River shipping companies have unanimously formed an alliance to

regulate the goods transported, calculating by cost for high-value goods and by weight for bulky goods. As a result, the Shanghai Suzhou goods merchants and others have united in opposition and adopted a policy of suspending shipments. Merchants have been struggling in the market for a long time without resolution. If this continues, both sides will suffer. We believe that with the bankruptcy of our country's rural areas and the declining purchasing power of the people, the economic downturn is a common phenomenon today. There is no reason why all industries are declining while the shipping industry alone can prosper. Our association has repeatedly received letters of appeal from various industries, so we are specially sending this letter to you. We hope that you will uphold the principle of coexistence and mutual prosperity and revise the freight rates properly with various merchant groups based on the old standards. We also hope that you will immediately restore the old shipping conditions. The Sichuan Shanghai Native Place Association.

Yuxing Delayed in Arriving in Shanghai 90

Damaged the Tong'an Warship in Qingdao

The Yuxing steamship of Zhaoxing Company, which had just undergone major repairs at the Lushun shipyard, loaded coal in Tianjin and arrived in Shanghai via Longkou, Yantai, Qingdao, and other ports. It arrived in Qingdao on the 18th and was scheduled to arrive in Shanghai yesterday. However, when the Yuxing steamship was leaving Qingdao,

due to the narrowness of Qingdao port, the *Tong'an* warship belonging to the Bohai Fleet was anchored in the harbor. The *Yuxing*, navigating carelessly, collided with the *Tong'an* warship, causing a major accident. The hull of the *Tong'an* warship was broken by the *Yuxing*.

Damaged Warship: After the accident, the *Yuxing* immediately stopped and dropped anchor. The owner of the *Yuxing*, together with the captain of the *Tong'an* warship, jointly inspected the damaged area to prepare for future repairs and negotiations. After the inspection, the *Yuxing* weighed anchor and left Qingdao for Shanghai, but it was delayed by one day.

Sailing to Yingkou Today: Yesterday afternoon, this port received news that the *Yuxing* steamship was generally undamaged and could enter the port today. It will first unload coal at the Hanyeping Wharf and then load cargo at the river wharf. Zhaoxing Company received a telegram from Yingkou yesterday stating that the weather there had warmed up, the ice had thawed, and ships could resume sailing. Cargo was waiting to be shipped from Yingkou, so it was decided that the *Yuxing* would resume sailing today. The cargo going from Shanghai consists mostly of flour, grains, foreign paper, tea, etc. This time, the *Yuxing* can be fully loaded. However, items such as cotton yarn and cloth are no longer shipped from Shanghai due to the high import duties imposed to support the inferior goods market.

Proposals from the employer side have been solicited by the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce from chambers of commerce in various regions and major factories in this port. All departure procedures have been completed.

The Rickshaw Issue is Becoming Increasingly Serious 92

Since Mr. Beck and others from the Western Rotary Club suggested reforming the issue of public rickshaws in the Public Concession, the Shanghai Municipal Council, in order to investigate and improve the rickshaw industry and provide relief to rickshaw pullers, established a rickshaw committee in September of last year, appointing three Western members and two Chinese members to conduct investigations for four months. The results, detailed in the Shanghai Municipal Council Gazette's special issue on rickshaws on the 23rd of this month, recommend sixteen innovative measures to reform the current public rickshaw system. The main measures include the annual confiscation of 2,000 of the existing 10,000 rickshaw operator licenses in the concession starting in January 1935, the establishment of a new operating company, the elimination of contractors, the reduction of rickshaw rentals from 14 cents to 8 cents per day per rickshaw, and the setting of minimum passenger fares at 10 cents, 20 cents per mile, and 60 cents per hour. These measures have aroused unanimous opposition from over 100,000 rickshaw operators, contractors, and rickshaw pullers in the city, who have risen up in protest, convened meetings, and organized countermeasures, creating a serious situation that has attracted attention from both Chinese and foreigners. The news from yesterday is summarized below.

Yin Zhiling Met with Mr. Bell to Discuss the Issue: The Shanghai Rickshaw Trade Association's Special District Office, in addition to issuing a declaration correcting the report and requesting the Municipal Council to pay attention to it, also held a general meeting of all rickshaw operators in the Special District at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the morning of the 14th of this month, attended by over 1,500 people. The report was unanimously recognized as having a plan to deprive rickshaw operators and cut off the livelihoods of rickshaw pullers under the guise of improving the rickshaw industry and providing relief to rickshaw pullers. They unanimously and resolutely opposed it. On the spot, Yin Zhiling, Gu Songmao, and others were elected to negotiate with the Municipal Council and issue a declaration and petition, stating six measures for rickshaw operators to automatically improve the rickshaw industry and provide relief to rickshaw pullers, including establishing rickshaw puller hospitals and new rickshaw puller villages. This has turned the rickshaw issue, which has been causing an uproar, into a social movement of extreme importance to improve the lives of over 100,000 laborers. Mr. Bell, the Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council, held a final review of the rickshaw report at a management meeting the night before and invited Yin Zhiling to the Chairman's office for a discussion at 3 p.m. Rickshaw Committee Chairman Mr. Massey was also present. The discussion is recorded below: (Bell asked) The Municipal Council will hold an important meeting regarding the rickshaw issue. I would like to hear about the rickshaw operators' license situation and their prices. (Yin replied) Rickshaw operators who change careers for various reasons will sell their vehicles, but there should absolutely be no buying and selling of licenses alone, so I will not answer the price question. (Asked) It is said that rickshaw operators sell their licenses for hundreds of yuan each and make a lot of profit. Is this proper? (Answer) Rickshaw operators who sell their vehicles may receive hundreds of yuan per vehicle, but only the former foreign-owned Flying Star Company has a payment plan where the rental fee is used to offset the vehicle price, so it can amount to four or five hundred yuan. On the Chinese side, there are few cases where a vehicle worth over one hundred yuan is bought and sold for four or five hundred yuan. (Asked) Is it untrue that the rickshaw committee's report stated that a former rickshaw operator said that the license was worth 650 yuan? (Answer) Everything said by that former rickshaw operator is an exaggeration, or it is a misunderstanding of the installment payment sale of vehicles. (Asked) What are the rickshaw operators' opinions on reducing rickshaw rentals? (Answer) The Rickshaw Committee suggests 8 cents per rickshaw per day, which should not be too difficult for rickshaw operators. However, the current system of renting out rickshaws is that contractors rent rickshaws from rickshaw companies under long-term contracts, with a rental fee of about 9 cents per rickshaw. The contractors then recruit rickshaw pullers, provide accommodation, and rent out the rickshaws to the rickshaw pullers for 13 or 14 cents per day. If the contractors only collect 8 cents per rickshaw rental from the rickshaw pullers, then the contractors will not only have no way to make a living but will also lose 1 cent per rickshaw per day. The contractors will inevitably be unable to provide rickshaw puller accommodation and loans, and rickshaw pullers will immediately face the risk of unemployment and being evicted by the contractors to collect debts. Rickshaw operators, due to contractual relationships, will also be unable to recover the rickshaws from the contractors for a while to rent them directly to rickshaw pullers. Even if this is feasible, it is doubtful whether rickshaw pullers can find other accommodation and repay the contractors' debts, freely renting rickshaws from rickshaw companies. Therefore, in order to reduce the burden on rickshaw pullers, it is necessary to provide them with accommodation so that they can break away from the contractor relationship and rent rickshaws directly from rickshaw companies. Before the above problems are resolved, a compromise should be made, setting 12 cents as the standard, so that the contractors will have 3 cents left after paying the rickshaw company 9 cents, which should be enough to cover their expenses. If the current rickshaw rental is 14 cents per day, it is hoped that it can be reduced by 2 cents, which will be a small help to the rickshaw pullers. Therefore, I believe that the methods passed by the rickshaw operators' conference to automatically improve rickshaws, provide relief to rickshaw pullers, and establish rickshaw puller villages are thorough methods to fundamentally alleviate the burden and all the suffering of rickshaw pullers. If rickshaw pullers live in the new villages, they will not only benefit from hygiene education and improve their lives, but they can also rent rickshaws directly from rickshaw companies and pay only 8 or 9 cents per day. (Asked) Why didn't rickshaw operators improve relief in the past, and are they confident in carrying out relief improvement in the future? (Answer) In the past, rickshaw operators operated in accordance with regulations, and the authorities did not stipulate relief matters, so they did not pay attention to it. Now, because the Rickshaw Committee's report recognizes that rickshaw pullers are in great need of relief and improved living standards, rickshaw operators are very willing to accept the Rickshaw Committee's goodwill for relief. The general meeting of all rickshaw owners has unanimously passed relief improvement methods and reported them to your bureau. They are determined and capable of implementing them. It is hoped that your bureau will guide the implementation at any time in a spirit of cooperation. (Asked) It is reported that Westerners in your bureau seem to be biased against the rickshaw issue. Is this true? (Answer) Since the publication of the Rickshaw Committee's report, there have been suggestions to establish a new company, abolish the contractor system, regulate fares, and...
