These measures concern the vital interests of rickshaw businesses, owners, headmen, and pullers. They are causing widespread panic. Rickshaw businesses are wary of the proposed new company structure, fearing that Westerners proposing improvements to rickshaws may be trying to seize their livelihoods. (Reports indicate that a British merchant has already petitioned the Public Works Department to establish a rickshaw company.) Rickshaw pullers question the proposed minimum fare of one "small ocean" dollar, noting that bus and tram fares start at only five or six copper coins, while rickshaws require twenty or thirty. They worry that passengers will switch to trams, harming the pullers' interests. Some suspect that these proposals are being pushed by tram and bus companies to expand their operations. However, the Human-Powered Vehicle Committee's recommendations may not necessarily reflect the views of your department. Therefore, external rumors of bias towards the proposals cannot be considered reflective of your department's attitude towards rickshaws until you have accepted and implemented them. In short, I have always been involved in education and social work. Having witnessed rural bankruptcy, I came to Shanghai to earn a living through labor. When there is no appropriate method to settle the lives of the hundred thousand rickshaw pullers, it's necessary to maintain the rickshaw industry, and it is not for the benefit of a few rickshaw owners, but for the sake of the lives of the majority of toiling pullers and social stability. From the perspective of social reform movements, helping rickshaw pullers requires not only reducing rent, but also effectively improving their lives, giving them a little common sense, so that they can work in other industries, then there will be no problem in eliminating the rickshaw industry. Therefore, I believe that the realization of the Rickshaw Pullers' New Village plan, the transformation of the rickshaw pullers' environment, and the influence of health education will not only make them physically and mentally healthy, but also eliminate the need for headmen to introduce rickshaw pullers, and allow them to seek other jobs when necessary. At that time, not only will the headman system be naturally abolished, but also the city's rickshaw companies will be naturally eliminated. I sincerely hope that your department and those who are interested in improving the rickshaw industry and rescuing rickshaw pullers will work together to promote and realize the Rickshaw Pullers' New Village plan. (Question) Very good, very good. Please also convey to the gentlemen of your association that this bureau deeply sympathizes with the cause of rescuing rickshaw pullers, has no other intentions, and no private agenda to deprive others of their livelihoods. It is hoped that this will not be misunderstood. (Answer) I am very grateful for your department's kindness in rescuing rickshaw pullers. The rickshaw merchants will certainly actively strive to build all kinds of undertakings for rescuing rickshaw pullers. Although there are many criticisms of the Human-Powered Vehicle Committee's report, its impact on the rickshaw merchants' desire to improve rickshaws and help rickshaw pullers is profound and significant. Therefore, I am very grateful to all the committee members for their deep concern for the rickshaw industry. I heard that after Dr. Yin resigned, Mr. Bell and Mr. MacKay went to the joint meeting of the police and vehicle departments and carefully studied the recommendations of the Human-Powered Vehicle Committee for up to six hours. It is said that as a result, for the sake of prudence, the board of directors was first asked to appoint three more committee members (two Chinese and one foreign) to study in detail how to implement items 4 to 16 of the proposal without being obstructed. Therefore, there is a tendency to implement it in a more relaxed manner.

Rickshaw Pullers' Union Letter to Rotary Club: The Shanghai Western Rotary Club had previously made suggestions to the concession authorities regarding the improvement of rickshaws. Yesterday, the Shanghai Concession Rickshaw Pullers' General Union sent a letter to the club, stating that the club's views did not fully understand the true situation of the rickshaw pullers. The letter read: "Dear Sirs, you have previously submitted a proposal to the authorities to improve public rickshaws, and have now expressed your sympathy for the recommendations of the Human-Powered Vehicle Committee, which shows your great concern for transportation and your compassion for laborers. If this is implemented, it will be thanks to your association's promotion that the workers will be able to improve their lives. We are grateful and immeasurably moved. However, we must speak out against the idea of gradually eliminating rickshaws as a means of abolishing inhumane practices. The rickshaw pullers come from the sea and are mostly rural people. They want to do business but have no capital, and they want to work but have no introduction. Their only job is pulling rickshaws, and they have no other skills. If rickshaws were to disappear one day, no matter how painful it would be for the rickshaw merchants and headmen, the hundred thousand rickshaw pullers and their families would inevitably lose their livelihoods and become starving corpses. How could we bear this? Therefore, we have sent this special letter to you, hoping that you will consider our plight and apply to the authorities to set up more factories and accommodate as many people as possible so that they can work and support themselves. If there is no way to settle us, please reconsider all proposals that imply the gradual elimination of rickshaws in order to maintain the livelihoods of the hundred thousand rickshaw pullers in the concession. This is our prayer. Respectfully to the Shanghai Western Rotary Club, from Chen Guorong, Hu Yucheng, He Songlin, Pan Jingang, Wang Dexi, Xu Chengsif, Xu Zhulin, Xu Zhaoyuan, Yao Shengting, Xu Chengyu, Pan Jinshu, and others, representatives of over eighty thousand rickshaw pullers in the Shanghai Public Concession."

The report has been carefully studied by the Police Committee and the Traffic Committee. Yesterday, the two committees continued to hold a joint meeting. It is reported that it was resolved to petition the Public Works Department to immediately appoint one foreigner and two Chinese to form a special committee to implement the recommendations in items 4 to 16 of the report. They will also apply for further research on these three articles when discussing the details of the implementation of the entire plan in the future. According to reports today (20th) from responsible parties, these three articles have not been abolished, because the Joint Committee of the Police and Traffic Committees felt that they could not make a final decision on this matter, so they thought it was appropriate to postpone it."

Navigation Notice: Shingle Slope Occurs in the Yangtze River 96

In the Waterway from Yanhu to Anqing

According to reliable information from the naval authorities in this city, the Ministry of the Navy reported that a shingle slope has occurred on the left bank of the Shiqiao Channel in the section of the Yangtze River from Wuhu to Anqing. The situation is as follows:

Direction: On the left bank of the Tuqiao Channel, (A) 44 degrees north from Baiwu, distance 125 nautical miles, (B) 77.5 degrees north from Baiwu, distance 54 chains (every 10 chains equals one nautical mile), east longitude approximately 117 degrees 43 minutes, north latitude approximately 31 degrees 2 minutes.

Shape: The shingle slope extends from the shoreline into the river, extending half a chain at location (I) and one chain at location (II). (III) Depth: When the river water falls to the zero point of the water gauge, the stone slope is two feet above the water surface. It is also known that after receiving the report, the Ministry of the Navy has issued a notice to inform navigators.

Requesting Tax Refunds for Wheat Flour Sold Abroad 97

Flour Manufacturers Petitioning the Ministries of Finance and Industry

Dagong News Agency reports: The Shanghai Flour Industry Association and the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Inland Mechanized Flour Industry Association yesterday submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, the Customs Administration, the National Tariff Commission, and other agencies, stating: "We are submitting this petition to request a refund of the imported wheat tax levied on wheat flour sold abroad and in the three northeastern provinces, in order to protect and promote competition. All countries in the world, in order to develop their foreign trade and encourage industrial and commercial enterprises, refund the imported raw material tariff to manufacturers whenever finished goods are sold abroad and the raw materials are purchased from abroad after being made into finished goods and reported for export. Also, the three northeastern provinces are the inherent sales market for flour factories across the country. Since your department ordered the Customs Administration to levy import taxes on foreign wheat, the cost of flour has increased, and its selling price is more than three jiao higher per bag than flour from Japan and Australia. Therefore, the sales in the three northeastern provinces have been completely cut off, and not even a single bag can be shipped. We are sitting idly by while Japanese and Australian flour is imported into the northeastern provinces, and we cannot compete with it. If we do not quickly seek a remedy, in the long run, not only will all of our country's flour factories inevitably shut down and reduce production, but also the government's tax revenue and the workers' livelihoods will be greatly affected. Our association has repeatedly discussed remedial measures, and the only option is to earnestly request your department to consider the commercial difficulties and follow the example of other countries in the world by refunding the imported wheat tariff already levied on the wheat flour produced by our association's factories when it is sold abroad and in the three northeastern provinces, in order to protect and promote competition. As for the tax refund method, it is proposed that the tariff levied on imported foreign wheat should be approximately 6.6 jiao in national currency per hundred catties, and each hundred catties of wheat can be processed into two bags of flour, then the import tariff on the raw material should be refunded at 3.3 jiao in national currency per bag of flour. The amount of tax refund should be limited to the amount of foreign wheat import tariffs paid by the manufacturers throughout the year. We earnestly request your department to approve our request, so that the production cost can be reduced and the sales channels can be competed for, so that there will be a glimmer of hope. The member factories of our association are eagerly awaiting your order. We respectfully submit this petition."

After the Cigarette Tax Reform, the Sales of Domestic Tobacco Leaves Have Sharply Decreased 100

Since the implementation of the new two-grade cigarette tax, the domestic cigarette industry has been greatly affected due to the heavy tax on low-grade cigarettes, which has affected the domestic tobacco leaves that are the raw material for domestic cigarettes. According to the Xinsheng News Agency's investigation, the domestic tobacco leaves produced in Susong, Anhui; Huanggang and Guangshui, Hubei; Xinchang, Zhejiang; and Zhengzhou, Guanjun, and Junzhou, Henan, sold approximately 390,000 bales per year during the seven-grade tax period before 1919 of the Republic of China, each bale weighing approximately 250 pounds. After the three-grade tax was changed in November 1919, the sales volume decreased to 265,000 bales per year. Since the implementation of the two-grade tax in 1922 of the Republic of China, the annual sales are now only 115,000 bales. In addition to the small amount of locally produced cigarettes and a small amount of exports, the various Chinese and foreign mechanized cigarette factories no longer purchase them due to the high price. From this, it can be seen that the improper change of tax grades affects the livelihoods of farmers. In addition, the American tobacco leaves of Xuzhou, Fangzi, and Fenghuang Sanhao will inevitably be eliminated by this tax increase.

The Chinese Chemical Industry Association Helps the Domestic Basic Industry 101

Petitioning for Increased Import Tariffs

The Chinese Chemical Industry Association, one of the well-known academic groups in China, aims to study chemical science and promote the chemical industry. Recently, in view of the basic chemical products imported from Europe, America, Japan, and Russia, such as soda ash, caustic soda, sodium sulfide, carbonic acid, calcium, magnesium sulfate, hydrochloric acid, bleaching powder, etc., the volume of goods shipped to China is like a tide, and the international exchange rate is low and the price of gold is falling, and the import tax is light, so low-price competition, a large number of dumping, and the cost of our basic industry is heavy, the selling price is low, and the market is lost, the future of national goods will be in danger, so the association's organization members Tianjin, Yongli Alkali Plant, Bohai Chemical Company, Shanghai Tianyuan Electrochemical Plant, Kaicheng Acid Company, etc., petitioned the Executive Yuan and the Legislative Yuan to implement tariff policies to increase the import tax on chemical products for relief.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Informs the Customs to Correct the Valuation Standard of Flour 102

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Jiang Customs Supervisor's Office yesterday requesting the correction of the valuation standard for flour exports. The original text reads: "Dear Sirs, according to the letter from the Flour Industry Association of this city, Mr. Zhao Shufang of the Laozuixiang Company, a member of the association, stated that the flour products of our industry have always been mainly aromatic powder oil, among which the sales of bottled powder are particularly widespread both domestically and abroad, and the four northeastern provinces are the most important markets. The raw materials used are purely domestic. The customs duty on goods is levied at 7.5%. However, customs officers increased the price to one silver cent per bottle (approximately 4.2 national currency cents). It is said that the customs officers inquired about the price in the Huajinli area. It is not known that the bottled powder in our industry has different prices for door-to-door sales and wholesale. The goods themselves are also different. Now, the valuation is more than doubled. Fortunately, the business was still good at that time, so we could bear the pain. Now, the situation has changed, and the business is declining. The four northeastern provinces are now occupied by the pseudo-Manchu. Sixty percent of the goods shipped there are subject to re-taxation. According to the customs valuation, a 60% tax is levied, resulting in a sharp increase in costs, and no one is advising us. Now, according to the joint announcement of the Hakka people in that area, we must seek help from each other at this time of national crisis. If the previously overvalued and falsely increased tariffs are not corrected, the sales channels will be cut off, and the future will be unimaginable. Therefore, we have made a special request for relief, requesting that the imaginary valuation be cancelled and that the bottled powder be allowed to be declared for export in accordance with the actual market price for tax payment, or that the invoice be presented for verification at the time of customs inspection, as a standard for valuation, so that it will be fair. If you are concerned about the credibility of this type of invoice, our association is willing to take full responsibility and provide a written guarantee, so that the country's taxes will not be hindered, and the business will be maintained, so that the surviving national flour can extend its life in the sunshine." According to the investigation, the sales of bottled aromatic powder in this industry are the most extensive in the four northeastern provinces. Now that they are occupied by the pseudo-Manchu,

a 60% ad valorem tax is levied on the import of this bottled powder, which is based on the price fixed by the Jiang Customs. And the price estimated by the Jiang Customs is still when the business is booming, regardless of the price of the door-to-door wholesale. According to the current market price, which is falling day by day, 60% of the estimated tax is levied on sales to the four northeastern provinces, no wonder its cost has suddenly risen, and the sales channel is in danger of disappearing. The industry association proposes to apply for certification and submit the invoice to the association to prove the standard of valuation, which is a fair and just proposal. Therefore, we hereby forward the information and request your office to verify it and quickly discuss it with the tax department and approve it as requested in order to maintain business.

Ministry of Communications Explains Three Measures to Ban Steamship Companies 103

Yesterday, the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau Was Ordered to Comply

The local Shipping Administration Bureau previously reported to the Wuhu Office requesting an explanation of the doubts about the measures to ban steamship companies. The bureau immediately forwarded the report to the Ministry of Communications for review. Now, it is known that the bureau received the following explanation from the Ministry of Communications yesterday: (1) The size of the shipping business is different, and the amount of capital is not limited. It should be determined according to the scope of the equipment and be sufficient for business use. Rental fees and docks are naturally part of the capital. If the competent shipping administration bureau considers it necessary to verify the deposit of the current capital in banks or money shops, it may verify it. The method of obtaining proof from three reliable local merchants may also be adopted. (2) Individuals engaged in shipping business should still be handled in accordance with the first item. (3) If the shipping route certificate has already been obtained, it is still valid if the original starting point is not followed and the intermediate point is used as the starting point. There is no need to change the shipping route certificate.

Silk Mills Open with No End in Sight: The Association to Aid the Unemployed Held a Meeting the Day Before Yesterday 104

It Was Decided to Petition the Party and Government

And Issued a Call for Assistance Declaration

The local silk reeling industry, due to the impact of Japanese silk dumping in Europe and the United States, silk prices have fallen and sales have been sluggish, making it difficult for the factories to maintain their operations and closing down one after another. More than 80,000 workers have suddenly become unemployed, and their livelihoods are in danger. After joint discussions by the silk reeling associations in various districts, the Association to Aid Unemployed Workers was established and held its first meeting the day before yesterday, and issued a call for assistance declaration. The details are as follows:

First Meeting: The silk reeling associations in various districts of this city, because the resumption of silk mills is uncertain, and the government's assistance has not yet been realized, the workers are unemployed and terrified, convened a joint meeting of the silk reeling associations in various districts, established the Association to Aid Unemployed Workers, and held the first meeting at 2:00 pm yesterday, with more than 20 people attending, discussing the following proposals: (1) Elected Chen Xiupu, Yuan Yunlong, Yang Gengti, Le Xiaorong, and Yang Shumei as standing committee members; (2) Scheduled the start of registration of unemployed workers; (3) The association's expenses will be shared by the various district associations; (4) Omitted; (5) Issued a call for assistance declaration; (6) Each group will start work from now on; (7) Scheduled to petition the party and government agencies to request the implementation of measures to aid the silk industry.

Call for Assistance Declaration: The Shanghai Silk Reeling Industry Association to Aid Unemployed Workers issued a call for assistance declaration: "Since the opening of the five ports, due to the economic aggression of the great powers, the passive development of international trade has been created. Comparing the value of imported and exported goods over the years, there has been no year without an import surplus from 35 years before the Republic of China to the present for more than 50 years. The number of funds flowing to foreign countries is countless. How can our country not have economic deficits and the people are poor and the treasury is exhausted? Fortunately, raw silk is the main export, and the annual export value often reaches 160 to 70 million taels of customs silver, recovering benefits, which is not insignificant. In the Tongzhi and Guangxu years of the late Qing Dynasty, Chinese silk accounted for more than seven tenths of the raw silk sold in various countries around the world, so in the past, the position of Chinese silk in the world market can be said to be unparalleled. However, since then, due to the competition of Japanese silk, its position has been deteriorating. Although the export quantity of Chinese silk increased to nearly 190,000 dan in 1918 of the Republic of China, its value is no longer the same as before. In recent years, not only has the value fallen sharply, but also the export quantity has been drastically reduced, almost reaching a state where no one cares. The mulberry fields are abandoned, and the silk mills are closed down. Alas, the decline of the silk industry is extreme. Today, not only has the hope of using raw silk as the only way to reduce the import surplus become a bubble, but also the millions of people across the country who directly and indirectly rely on the silk industry for their livelihoods, how can they be well taken care of in the future? At present, no less than 60,000 to 70,000 unemployed workers in Shanghai are engaged in the silk mill business, waiting to be fed, and not guaranteeing the evening if they have a morning. If they do not quickly seek relief, the weak will wait to die, and the strong will take risks. Who can guarantee that there will be no such thing? If this continues, how can the social order and the economy of the common people be imagined? Although the National Economic Commission has organized a Silk Improvement Committee, it should be a fundamental solution to save

the silk industry, but what can be done about the water far away cannot put out the fire near? Therefore, the implementation of the policy of curing the symptoms by the administrative authorities is an urgent request of our workers and cannot be delayed. At the same time, we also hope that our compatriots at home and abroad will lend a helping hand, so that tens of thousands of workers and friends will not starve to death, and the country and society will benefit. When the association was first organized, I would like to say a few words as a dying cry and call for Jiang Bo. I hope you will take it into consideration. This is the declaration."

Due to the British Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Gonghe steamer renovating the officer cabins into large second-class dining rooms and hiring Western stewards, the original officer cabin workers felt that the cabins were small and the jobs were few, affecting their livelihoods. When the ship departed from Shanghai last time, twelve people were pushed out to automatically participate in the second-class dining room, causing a dispute. It is learned that the company, considering the workers' enthusiastic participation in the second-class dining room work and being eager to resolve the issue and respect the union, has softened its attitude. Yesterday, it specially urged Secretary Sun Liping of the union by telephone to come to the company for consultation. General Manager Tude and Chief Inspector Bu Ermo received him. After mutual discussion, it was decided that the second-class dining room of the ship will use people from the stewards and officer cabin workers in equal proportions. However, the title of the workers dispatched from the officer cabins will still be called mess staff and cannot be called stewards, in order to distinguish them. As for the total number of people to be used, it has not yet been discussed at this time.

Page 11

Climate Changes in the City, Gale Howls, Tumble-Down Wall of the Bowling Alley Collapses 110

Traffic Blocked on Nanjing Road for 20 Minutes

Three Men and One Woman Injured, One Rickshaw Destroyed

In the past few days, the weather in this port has been unusually cold, like severe winter weather. On the 18th and 19th, it suddenly turned warm again, with a gentle breeze blowing, like the season of early spring. However, those who suffered from diseases due to the abnormal climate were everywhere, especially the prevalence of smallpox and diphtheria. Unexpectedly, by yesterday afternoon, the weather changed again. Rain fell lightly. Condition of the Tumble-Down Wall of the Bowling Alley (Photo by Qichang)

The north wind howled, and compared with the temperature in the previous days, the difference reached ten degrees. By 6 PM, a sudden hurricane arose, and the roads were muddy. Therefore, pedestrians who lost their footing and fell to the ground, as well as those who lost their hats and umbrellas, could be seen everywhere. There were also countless shop signs on various roads that were blown down. Rickshaw pullers were all complaining bitterly. By 6:20 PM, the momentum was even greater. Where the hurricane passed, it howled, and trees were broken and walls collapsed. At 6:25 PM, just as the gale was howling, the cement parapet on the roof of No. 121, Shenchang Watch & Clock General Store, No. 129, Shichangtai General Store (i.e., the entrance of Ciyu Lane), No. 133, No. 135, Datong Leather Shoe Factory, and No. 137, No. 139, Xiao Lüsong Hat Cleaning General Store, all properties of Hardoon Foreign Firm at the bowling alley on Nanjing Road, collapsed from the highest point with a roar due to years of disrepair and severe erosion. For a time, bricks and tiles flew together, and the momentum was like a landslide and tsunami. The traffic in that section was immediately blocked by cement bricks and ash. At the same time, men Lu Xingzhi, 32 years old, Cao Songcai, 21 years old, shoemaker Wang Jindi, 26 years old, and a woman passed by on the sidewalk and were injured by the cement bricks. There was also a rickshaw parked by the roadside that was destroyed. Fortunately, the Central Police Station learned of this and immediately dispatched a large number of Chinese and foreign detectives to suppress the situation and prohibit traffic. They also notified the Central Fire Brigade to send firefighters and ambulances to help the injured out and send them to Renji and other hospitals for treatment. Except for shoemaker Wang Jindi, who was seriously injured in the head and waist and was hospitalized for treatment, the others were slightly injured and left the hospital after being bandaged. On the one hand, the firefighters quickly cleared the road, and by 7:20 PM, traffic was restored. All the trams, cars, and buses stopped along Nanjing Road from the east to the Bund Waibaidu Bridge and west to the New World had been winding like long snakes for about ten minutes before returning to normal. However, the wind had not subsided slightly by the time the reporter finished writing.

County Government Orders Districts to Open Rural Loan Programs 112

The Shanghai County Rural Improvement Association, in order to assist farmers' economy and promote the development of production undertakings, has set up a rural loan office. It has raised a principal of 3,000 yuan, which will be distributed to various districts. Each district will be allocated a provisional principal of 500 yuan, which will be received and lent out by the districts. If it is managed effectively, it will be expanded. Kang Jimin has been appointed as the director of the office, and the heads of each district will be the directors of the branch offices. The county government has now approved the association's letter to the county, so it issued an order to each district yesterday to prepare for the establishment of loan branch offices and handle the matter conscientiously. It is reported that this loan is divided into two types: ordinary and special. The ordinary loan is from one yuan to ten yuan, and the special loan shall not exceed fifty yuan per household. If the farmer has legitimate uses, he may seek a reputable guarantor to apply for a loan. However, the special loan must have considerable collateral, with a monthly interest rate of 1.2%, calculated daily.

Small Shop Assistant Pretends to Be a Great Lawyer 113

Hu Minggao Pretends to Be Wu Zhifen, Passing Off One Thing for Another

Extortionate Demands and Fraudulent Practices Exposed and Reported

Hu Minggao, from Chongming Qidong County, is 47 years old this year. He used to work as a shop assistant at Wang Zhidai's small cigarette and paper shop opposite the Puyi Skills Training Center on Nanshi Railway Station Road. In his spare time, he wrote guarantees and other documents for litigants. Over time, he became familiar with litigation procedures, so he left Wang Zhidai and rented a room under the Tongchun Tea House at No. 7 Tingxi Road, specializing in soliciting lawsuits and making friends with bailiffs and clerks to facilitate connections. His livelihood was not bad. However, Hu was still not satisfied. He learned that the lawyer's license and certificate of Wu Zhifen, a lawyer from Jing County, Anhui (whether he changed to another business or passed away is unknown), were sold to Hu Shi Gao through an intermediary. Thus, he was able to impersonate him and jump to become a lawyer. In July of last year, he asked four people, including his fellow villager, lawyer Yin Long, to help him provide a certificate so that he could join the Shanghai Bar Association. He still hung his signboard at the original address and performed his duties. Since then, his business has become even more prosperous. Recently, because Hu made excessive demands while handling a certain case and practiced fraudulent means under the guise of "movement," the client was deeply dissatisfied and secretly reported to the District Court Procuratorate Hu's impersonation and extortionate fraud and other secret history. Chief Prosecutor Lou knew that this person was often in front of the court and feared that he might leak information and escape. Therefore, he immediately secretly sent a letter to the Second District Police Station of the Public Security Bureau, requesting his arrest. District Chief Li secretly dispatched detectives who went to No. 7 Tingxi Road the night before last without making a sound, arrested Hu Minggao, and brought back his signboard and documents to the district. After a brief interrogation, he was transferred to the local court yesterday for interrogation and investigation.

Zhang Zhuying's Son Da Yuan Is Born to Zhou Yuexuan 114

Da Yuan's Blood Is the Same as Zhang and Zhou's

Verified by the Forensic Laboratory

Zhou Yuexuan, the eldest son of Zhou Weisheng, the owner of Zhou Gengji Yarn Shop, a wealthy merchant from Suzhou residing in Shanghai, once had a free love affair with Zhang Zhuying and lived together in a rented house at No. 8 Xinglongfang, Danshui Road. Soon, a son was born, named Da Yuan. However, before long, Zhou Weisheng learned of it and dissolved the small family formed by his son. Yuexuan, fearing the strict order, had no choice but to separate from Zhuying. The child was raised by Zhang, and the necessary living expenses each month were provided by Yuexuan until last autumn. Da Yuan was already eight years old when Yuexuan suddenly stopped paying the monthly fee, causing the child's life to become unstable. The child's mother, Zhang Zhuying, then filed a criminal lawsuit against Zhou Yuexuan for malicious abandonment in the First Special District Court on behalf of her child. After repeated summons and trials, the defendant categorically denied having a physical relationship with Zhang Zhuying. Trial Judge Wu Xiangzu, in order to discover the truth and avoid injustice, issued a notice to the forensic examination on file. It is now learned that the First Special Court has sent Zhang Zhuying, Zhou Yuexuan, and Da Yuan to the Forensic Research Institute of the Ministry of Justice Administration in Zhenru for examination according to law. The director of the institute, Lin Ji, made a register of the examination results and replied to the court. The content generally stated that Da Yuan's blood was completely the same as that of Zhou Yuexuan and Zhang Zhuying, and Da Yuan's appearance and bone structure were mostly very similar to Yuexuan and slightly similar to Zhang Zhuying, confirming that the child was indeed born to Zhou and Zhang. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu held a court session to continue the trial. First, he handed the examination report from the Forensic Research Institute to the defendant Zhou Yuexuan in court for review. Zhou then said that he had never had a relationship with Zhang and was surprised that the institute's appraisal showed that the child was born to him. Then he said that we are all yellow people, and our appearances are naturally mostly the same. If Da Yuan's blood is similar to mine, and it is determined that Da Yuan was born to me, then Zhang Zhuying and I have no father-daughter relationship, so why is our blood the same? The court considered that the defendant's argument was mere words. Therefore, it was ordered that if he wanted to deny it, he should submit definite evidence to the contrary. At this time, the defendant's lawyer requested a new appraisal and raised the issue of the jurisdiction of the trial level, saying that although the plaintiff's prosecution articles belonged to the primary level, the nature of the case was a local case. Judge Wu made an oral ruling, believing that there was no need for a new appraisal, and the issue of the trial level was still to be tried as a primary-level case, and there was no reason for change. Then, after re-examining Zhang Zhuying's time of birth of Da Yuan, and because the witnesses summoned had not arrived, he ordered that the hearing be rescheduled for the afternoon of March 31.

Dr. Ding Jinan's Car Accident Case 116

Although he was unwilling to accept the judgment, the legal proceedings of the case had come to an end, and there was no way to provide relief. Therefore, the Wen'an Prison incident, which had caused a sensation for a time, has come to an end.

Boxer Shen Buyun Loses His Life in a Fight 118

Instigator Surrenders to Police Station

Shen Buyun, a Tianjin native residing at No. 178 Huixiang Lane, Xilu, Xieqiao, Huajie, 31 years old, was skilled in boxing and made a living by performing. His business card, which he used for daily meetings, was printed with "Martial Arts Teacher of Yadon Middle and Small Day and Night School." He cohabited with a woman surnamed Tang (30 years old this year) from Songjiang. Shen, at 8:30 PM on the 18th, at the invitation of his friend Lü Wencai, also known as "Little Sanzi," brought his son's toys and went to the entrance of the Jiangbei Theater in the Minyeyuan at No. 86, Forty Head, Dushanfu Road, French Concession, to fight with someone. At that time, there were more than 20 people who had been invited to the scene by both sides, and the crowd was noisy and caused a great stir among the onlookers. Unexpectedly, although Shen called himself a martial arts teacher, he was struck in the head, right forehead, and back of the head by the other party with a triangular iron rod. Detectives heard the noise and rushed to disperse the onlookers and arrest the perpetrators. When the people from both sides and their accomplices saw the detectives arriving, they all fled from the crowd. Shen also fled back to his home at this time. However, the patrolman in the crowd saw that Liu Fugui (24 years old), from Shandong, was still holding an iron rod in his hand, knew that he was the perpetrator, and arrested him and took him to the police station for interrogation. Liu denied instigating the fight. The police chief ordered him to be detained for investigation and to arrest the fleeing accomplices for interrogation. However, after Shen returned home, his injuries became serious. The next day (19th) at about 8 AM, his wife, Tang, accompanied him to Baolong Hospital on Baker Road, Public Concession, for treatment. He died at 2:30 PM due to excessive head injuries, and the hospital reported to the Xinza Police Station, which notified the French Police Station to send detectives to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch for autopsy. On the one hand, detectives went to the scene of the incident to investigate the circumstances of the fight. At 5 PM, Lü Wencai, who had invited Shen to fight, learned of Shen's death and surrendered to the French Police Station for investigation. Yesterday morning, the police station reported to the Procuratorate of the Second Special District Court and requested the appointment of Prosecutor Wang Ren and forensic officers to come to the hall at noon to verify the body and ascend to the public case. First, Patrol Chief Chang Chunsheng reported on the investigation process. Shen Tang, the wife of the deceased, testified that her husband had gone out at about 8 PM that evening, saying he was going to the theater, and did not mention anything about going to fight. At 9 PM, he returned home injured. When I asked him, he said that someone was fighting and he went up to dissuade them, resulting in him being injured. The next day, I accompanied him to the hospital for treatment, but he died. Now I am willing to collect the body for burial. Prosecutor Wang verified the testimony and ordered that Shen Buyun had indeed died due to injuries sustained before death. The body was collected by the deceased's wife, Shen Tang, for burial, and the perpetrators should be dealt with by the Police Department according to law. It is rumored that wanted criminal Yang Dafuzi is at large and has not been apprehended. Now, the police are conducting a thorough investigation into the truth of the incident and arresting the perpetrators.

Forging as Many as 50,000 Cigarette Coupons 119

Yu Azhang Exchanges for Three Cups Brand Cigarettes at Cigarette Shops Everywhere

Several Thousand Packs of Cigarettes Have Been Exchanged Before Being Cracked the Other Day

Recently, Dexing Tobacco Company on Zhejiang Road issued a type of Three Cups Brand cigarette coupon. Anyone who obtains a coupon can exchange it for a box of Three Cups Brand cigarettes at any cigarette shop. Unexpectedly, A'zhang, Shi Wangshi, Shi Xixiang, Fang Changfu, and others from Ningbo recently contracted with a printing house to print forged coupons, totaling 50,000. They also forged the official seal of Dexing Tobacco Company. In recent days, they have set out separately, carrying forged coupons, to mix in various cigarette shops in the Chinese and rental districts. However, the cigarette shops were negligent for a while, and the coupons were well-made, so they were deceived. In the past few days, Yu and others have used thousands of forged coupons to exchange for thousands of packs of cigarettes. At about 9 PM the day before yesterday, Shi Xixiang and Fang Changfu were again carrying rattan baskets and hiding forged coupons, starting to mix in various cigarette shops in the Public Concession. When they went to Futa Cigarette Shop at No. 131 Changsha Road to use them, the shop's bookkeeper, Shao Minggeng, noticed that the coupons were forged. Therefore, he argued with Shi and others. At that time, Ma Shicai, a runner for Dexing Tobacco Company, passed by and asked about the situation and confirmed that the coupons were indeed forged. Therefore, he reported to Chinese Patrolman No. 905, who brought Shi and Fang to the Xinza Police Station. Chief Chinese Detective Su Yinggen and Patrolman Yang Youshan searched Shi and found 25 forged coupons and one genuine coupon. They searched the rattan basket and found 216 packs of Three Cups Brand cigarettes. They then joined forces with detectives from the Public Security Bureau to arrest Yu Azhang and Shi Wangshi at No. 102 Dajing Road, Xiaobeimen, Nanshi. More than 40,000 forged coupons were found upstairs and temporarily detained at the Public Security Bureau, pending a written request for transfer. Yesterday morning, the police station first sent Shi and Fang to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Jiang Baolian stated the case, saying that there were still Yu Azhang and Yu Wangshi, who were currently detained at the Public Security Bureau, and requested a written request for transfer. Questioning Shi and Fang, they admitted that Yu Azhang was involved in the forged coupons. Judge Wu Tingqi verified the testimony and ordered Shi and others to be detained for a retrial at a later date.

Municipal Party Headquarters Strictly Order the Prohibition of Ferry Workers' Union Activities 120

Willing to be Exploited by Local Bullies to Maintain Private Interests

Undermining the Establishment of Ferry Services, Disregarding Public Welfare

国民社 reports that the Municipal Government, for the sake of facilitating public travel, intends to establish ferry services at Dongjiadu. This time, the Municipal Government's establishment of ferry services is based on the request of the people of the district, to facilitate public travel. Unexpectedly, the original boatmen and workers of the ferry are ignorant and foolish, rising up in opposition, willingly being exploited by local bullies, attempting to undermine the establishment of ferry services, maintaining private interests, and disregarding public welfare, which is entirely inappropriate. In addition to separate orders to the First and Fifth District Party Headquarters, it is urgently ordered that the union comply, quickly jointly prohibiting the boatmen and workers of the ferry from being exploited by others to oppose the establishment of ferry services, and they are not allowed to use the name of the union to assemble, petition, or incite disturbances, so as to benefit the municipality. Upon receipt of this order, act immediately, without any delay or mistake, this order is imperative."

The Public Works Department and Industry Within the Settlement 121

Work Report for the Previous Year

Negotiations Stalled The Public Works Department of the Shanghai International Settlement, in its work report for the previous year, mentioned the state of industry within the settlement. It stated, "Since 1931, when the Chinese government announced the implementation of the Factory Law, the Public Works Department also declared its principled support for the industrial management. Subsequently, two representatives from the International Labour Office came to Shanghai, and the Ministry of Industry invited representatives from the three municipal districts of Shanghai to informally consult on everything. In 1932, due to the situation, progress came to a halt. In March of last year, the Director-General of the Public Works Department and the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government discussed the issue of factory inspections. The Public Works Department, based on the consultations of 1931, put forward three points: 1) The Public Works Department is prepared to employ factory inspectors recommended by the Chinese government; 2) Inspection reports will be submitted to the Chinese government on a regular basis, in accordance with the agreed-upon format; 3) The inspectors from the three municipal districts can agree to meet once a month. However, the government's 'supervision' of inspectors within the settlement should not include jurisdictional authority, and the correspondence between the inspectors and the government should be forwarded through the Public Works Department." This proposal was not agreed to by the Chinese side. Later, it was discussed to form an inspection office, jointly directed by the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government and the Director-General of the Public Works Department, but the board of directors believed that the jurisdiction of the inspectors could not be divided, so it was not accepted either. After mid-October, these negotiations came to a standstill.

Accident Incidents Statistics for the first eight months of the previous year regarding industrial accident incidents within the settlement show 163 workers injured and 120 killed, totaling 283 people. Among them, 155 were male and 128 were female. The biggest cause of death and injury was explosions, with 44 deaths and injuries; falls accounted for 48; electricity, 19; fire, 19; and contusions, 18. Among them, 42 were construction workers. Factory fires accounted for 28.15% of the fires within the settlement, and the fire losses accounted for 49.9% of the total amount.

Suppressing Construction Because smaller factories within the settlement have difficulty obtaining land, there are frequent cases of converting alleyway houses into factories, resulting in various dangers. The Public Works Department has now notified those applying for Chinese-style housing licenses that they are not allowed to add or demolish walls without authorization. The construction or reconstruction of factories will be strictly inspected by the Works Department at any time. In addition to the construction of houses, the Public Works Department will pay attention to the electrical installations and equipment containing pressure components in the factories in order to reduce danger.

The Two-Roads Administration Responds to the Chamber of Commerce Regarding the Relocation of the Panjiwan Wooden Bridge 122

The Two-Roads Administration yesterday replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating, "Having received your letter 商字 No. 805, regarding the preservation of the wooden bridge at the east end of the Zhabei Bridge, this Bureau has successively received petitions from merchants and residents in the area and instructed the Vehicle, Mechanical, and Engineering Departments to deliberate and respond, stating, 'The addition of a concrete wall from Maigen Road to Bridge No. 1 is being carried out under the Bureau's order. There are three necessary reasons: 1) Without a wall, it is difficult for road police to investigate and prevent thieves from mixing into the Maigen Road warehouses; 2) According to statistics from the Vehicle Department, an average of one ignorant and foolish person is crushed to death by trains each month for taking the small wooden bridge; 3) The shanties of the poor encroach on the road boundaries, creating filth and mess, which must be blocked by a wall. If we follow the request of the shops, the original intention of adding the wall will be completely ineffective. Also, the area along Jiaotong Road is full of factories and residents. Most of those who travel between Panjiwan and Jiaotong Road are ordinary people and small workers. Before January 28th, vendors and small shops were all set up on Jiaotong Road, so fewer people traveled across the small wooden bridge. Now, as a result of police intervention, they have all moved to Bridge No. 1 south of the railway tracks, so even more people travel across the small wooden bridge every day. However, if the residents of Panjiwan take Tanziwan Road, they can also reach Jiaotong Road. Therefore, we believe the best solution is for the shops to request the Shanghai Municipal Government to build a bridge south of Railway Bridge No. 1, across the Suzhou Creek, and open a road from this bridge to Tanziwan Road. This Bureau has a half-traffic point on Tanziwan Road, so people traveling through this point can pass through the tracks without danger. Before this plan is realized, it is proposed to temporarily move the current small wooden bridge to a point 10 meters away from Railway Bridge No. 1, and build an underground passage on the east bank, passing through the railway, to maintain traffic in the Panjiwan area. We await your inspection and verification as to whether this is appropriate." After reviewing the above, the proposed measures are appropriate. In addition to instructing that the proposal be approved, and separately replying to the merchants and residents, this letter is accordingly delivered, hoping you will investigate and comply accordingly."

Extending the Free Storage Period for Goods 124

Seven-Day Free Storage Implemented Starting Yesterday

The Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) and Huhangyong (Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo) Railways Administration, regarding the free storage period for goods stored in railway warehouses by merchants, extended it from 24 hours to 7 days in mid-June of last year, and appropriately reduced the storage fees for overdue goods. When the two-month trial period ended in mid-September, it was again approved by the Ministry of Railways to extend the period for six months. Subsequently, due to the fact that the Maigen Road warehouse was completely full, in order to alleviate congestion, it was decided that from November 3rd, the free storage period for goods in that warehouse would be temporarily changed from 7 days to 5 days, and the storage fees for fourth-class and lower-class goods would also be temporarily charged at the rate of third-class goods (5 fen per ton per day). Now, the Railway Administration has approved the return of the free storage period for all goods arriving at the Maigen Road warehouse to 7 days. After this specified date, the storage fee rates for fourth-class and lower-class goods, which were originally charged at the rate of third-class goods, will be changed to be calculated according to the original grade, that is, 5 li per 50 kilograms or less for less-than-carload shipments, and 2.5 li per ton for carload shipments, effective from March 20th.

Public Settlement Fire Administration in February 125

The report of the Director of the Fire Department of the Public Works Department for the month of February states that a total of 82 alarms were received during the month, of which 5 were false alarms. The property endangered by fire was 2,218,575 taels within the settlement and 42,430 taels in the Special Donation Area. The actual losses were 37,864 taels and 7,610 taels respectively. Two people died in the fire, and 15 were injured. Seven firefighters were injured. The Fire Department's emergency ambulance responded 224 times, transporting 250 people to the hospital. The medical department's car transported a total of 266 patients.

A Big Fire on Haig Road Yesterday Morning 133

At around 0:30 yesterday morning, for some unknown reason, a fire suddenly broke out in the Wang Hongji barrel shop opened by Qingpu native Wang Hongquan at No. 1918 Haig Road, north of the gate of Jiaotong University in western Shanghai. Wang Quan's family was awakened from their dreams, but the fire was already very fierce and could not be controlled. It immediately spread to the homes of Ningbo native Zhang Jinlin at No. 1916, Tongzhou native Lu Agou and Huangyan native Chen Dexin at No. 1920, Tongzhou native Lu Genbin at No. 1922, the bamboo shop opened by Jiading native Chen Yusheng at No. 1924, the Nanfuxing restaurant opened by Taicang native Wu Guisheng at No. 1926, and Tang Abao, a small businessman from Changzhou, who lived with them, totaling 12 families. Later, Zhao Dianqing, the police chief of the Hongqiao Road Police Station of the 2nd branch of the 6th district in charge, learned about it and sent police to the fire to suppress it, and also notified the fire brigade by telephone to drive to the scene to put out the fire. Because the rear were all shanties, it was not easy to extinguish it for a while. It took more than an hour to extinguish it, but five tiled bungalows and more than ten shanties were burned, and the loss should be more than 5,000 yuan. Wang Hongquan, who started the fire, was taken back to the station and sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday for interrogation.

Letter to the Editor 142

To the editor,

According to the advertisements in various newspapers on the 10th of this month, the notice of the Shanghai Office of the China Aviation Association for soliciting captains of the general team included a list of teams that had not paid their donations in full. It stated that Lu Wenshao, captain of the third team, had raised 1,000 yuan but had not yet paid it. It has been verified that Mr. Lu previously donated 5,000 yuan for the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce aircraft to this association, and he did not intend to donate this amount. This matter was approved by a letter from the office on July 28th of the previous year, inquiring whether Mr. Lu had remitted the 1,000 yuan he had pledged to donate to the association. After inquiring about Mr. Lu's opinion, a letter No. 321 of the Pu character was sent in reply. This is obviously inconsistent with the sections reported by the office, which is likely to cause misunderstandings among outsiders. It is necessary to make a factual correction. Now, according to Mr. Lu's request to send a letter on his behalf to clarify the foregoing, in addition to sending a letter to the office requesting correction, we also request that your newspaper disclose this letter to clarify the truth. We hope for this.

Sincerely,

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, March 20, 23rd year [of the Republic].

Reading Q&A

How to Study the Northeast Problem 143

Reading Guidance Department:

Your department is responsible for guiding all young people—not only guiding readers, but also guiding the resolution of all practical problems. Therefore, I would like to propose this already forgotten but most important issue—the Northeast problem—and ask your department to propose an open discussion.

Japan's military occupation of the Northeast has become a thing of the past. Now it has begun a "root and branch" extermination policy. Japan is implementing this policy by many means. Due to space limitations, I can only write down a few of the most vicious means below.

(1) Implementing National Subjugation Education

Japan wants to make the 30 million people of Northeast China its slaves forever. The first thing to do is to implement slave education. Most of the universities and middle schools in the Northeast have been closed, and the elementary schools are only half-dead. The education departments of the provinces of the Northeast have set up curriculum editing committees to compile national subjugation textbooks. There are now many publications, the content of which is completely麻醉ideology to eliminate the soul. Japanese language is added for several hours a week in all elementary and middle schools. Japanese people are hired as teachers, in name as teachers, but in reality to supervise whether there are any anti-Japanese or anti-Manchu actions. If this continues, in five or ten years, the youth of the Northeast will not only not know how to love the country and save the country, but will also be completely Japanized and forget their motherland.

(2) Oppressing Intellectuals

Japan is even more cruel to intellectuals, using "dropping stones down a well." After the Incident, most intellectuals fled and disappeared, and news of open and secret killings was heard every day. Japanese plainclothes detectives are all over the cities of the Northeast, arbitrarily going to homes to search and inspect. Even if they find a magazine, you will be falsely accused of being a reactionary and arrested and imprisoned. As a result, all books have been burned clean. Some escaped intellectuals have also fled east and west, displaced. All that remains are some muddle-headed fools. Japan has also used various threats and oppressions against them to make them forget their motherland. A puppet emperor was established to 麻醉them. How can these fools, full of feudal ideas, see through this trick?

(3) Forcibly Eliminating the Volunteer Army

After the "September 18th" Incident, the Volunteer Army in the Northeast rose up like a storm, almost everyone was a soldier, and no one was not brave. Full of𤍠blood, they confronted the Japanese soldiers, who were well-equipped with精and彈, with bare hands. But now they are dying one by one. Their power is diminishing day by day. Although there are some remnants, they are also on their last breath, living from day to day. In order to completely eliminate the Volunteer Army, Japan has stationed strong troops in various places, and ordered that no tall sorghum crops be planted within 60 li of the railway line to prevent the Volunteer Army from hiding. The strictness of the measures can be described as meticulous. The Volunteer Army, which is enough to kill Japan, is probably about to be eliminated soon!

(4) Implementing a Poisoning Policy

Japan wants to make the 30 million people of the Northeast its slaves forever, so it implements a poisoning policy. It forces various places to plant opium. Since the "September 18th" Incident, the general farmers have seen the bankruptcy of the countryside and the failure to recover. In order to make a living, they have no time to consider the pros and cons, and they are all competing to plant opium. It is heard that the area planted has accounted for about 10% of the cultivated land. Since planting is officially allowed, smoking is naturally open. There are more than a thousand opium dens in major cities in the Northeast. Each opium den hires female attendants to serve smokers, and outside hires ruffians to "attract customers." In the streets and alleys, there are cries such as "The opium is delicious" and "The female attendants are beautiful." In order to implement the "addiction to smoking and sex" strategy, Japan clearly allows opium dens to openly accommodate smokers, just like brothels. Generally, young people who are not addicted to smoking are also addicted to sex. They lie in bed all day long, playing the flute, their ambitions are becoming more and more depressed, and their bodies are becoming weaker and weaker. Japan is only using this poisoning policy, which is enough to control the death of our 30 million compatriots in the Northeast and more! How painful!

Based on the above vicious means, Japan has made the greatest determination to destroy the Northeast. In order to maintain "territorial integrity," we should fight him to the death, but the opposite is true. We only see champagne celebrations and puppet ascensions, and we do not ask about the detailed plan for resisting Japan. As for the people, what about them? Recalling the time of the "September 18th" Incident, the whole country was boiling and the people were extremely激昂. The cry of "Resisting Japan and saving the country" was deafening. Strikes, market closures, petitions, and donations were all like "hitting the three ghost islands with one cannon and drinking a cup of wine in Huanglong." After a few days of commotion, the flags and drums were silenced, and the atmosphere was peaceful again. Movie theaters were full, and a film could be shown continuously for more than a month, and it was crowded every time. How prosperous it can be said! High-class Chinese people are high夫during the day and foxtrotting at night, clearly a "prosperous and peaceful country" that has no "national crisis" look. The government is so perfunctory, and the people's spirit is so depressed. Can the future still be imagined!

Editors: I cannot bear to see the country broken without resistance and the home lost without a price. I cannot bear to hear the heartbreaking cries of 30 million compatriots in the deep water. I want to take my whole life, a腔𤍠blood, and join comrades to save the Northeast, and make it my lifelong career, and do it without loosening a step. I now want to bury myself in the study of the Northeast problem thoroughly, as a south針for future work. But the Northeast problem is not a simple problem! Its outbreak was not accidental. My lack of knowledge and weak ability make me feel difficult about this problem. However, my ambition has been decided, and I cannot挫去it even a little because of the difficulty. I dare to ask your department to help me achieve my ambition and give me a helping hand, and guide me in detail to a research path. I am waiting earnestly for your reply. (A letter from Fang Juemeng, a refugee from the Northeast)

Spring and Autumn

Goldfish and the Two Sus 145

— Zhanlu

▼ Su Zimei waited for goldfish all day long

.▼ Su Dongpo considered it an honor to see golden carp in Nanping

The goldfish that modern people see are not uncommon. Before the Song Dynasty, no one played with them. Although Tang Dynasty officials had the title of "赐紫金鱼袋" [bestowed purple gold fish pouch], the purple gold fish pouch hanging on the waist was only a kind of "彰君之宠" [showing the emperor's favor] like jade fish and golden turtle pendants, and it was absolutely different from the goldfish that are played with now.

Now, even three-year-old children know goldfish; the ancients were not like that. Su Zimei and Su Dongpo in the Northern Song Dynasty were both regarded as learned gentlemen; who knows, when they saw golden carp, it was like a country bumpkin touring the Shanghai Bund, with a great look of "never seen before." Su Zimei even wanted to see goldfish and waited respectfully by the bridge all day long; forty years later, Su Dongpo read Su Zimei's two lines of poetry, "waiting for golden carp by the bridge, lingering alone all day long," and he was a bit inexplicable about the words "golden carp." Later, he went to the place where Zimei wrote poetry—the Liuhe Pagoda Temple—and saw golden fish in the pond, and he knew the origin of the words "golden carp." Dongpo was extremely happy. Not only did he describe this in Dongpo's poetry talks, but he also had a proud poem that said, "I know the golden carp of Nanping." Something that modern three-year-old children know, Su Dongpo composed poems about, and considered it an honor to know it. This is because of the times, and we cannot laugh at him for being 少见多怪 [seeing little and marveling at much].

Books recording goldfish all say: "The practice of raising goldfish became popular after the Southern Song Dynasty." Therefore, people in the Northern Song Dynasty always regarded the knowledge of goldfish as something surprising. Su Zimei was the first to appreciate goldfish, and more than forty years later, Su Dongpo followed. Apart from the two Sus, it would be very difficult to find a few poems about goldfish among the people of the Northern Song Dynasty.

Goldfish gardens are also one of the three hundred and sixty trades. Since there is a trade, there should be a respected patriarch. I think Su Zimei can be the founding patriarch of the goldfish industry. As for other people to be worshipped, old beard uncle Su Dongpo is 大槪 [probably] not un祧 [removed from the ancestral tablet].

Returning from Hongqiao Airfield 146

— Nanhai Shagou

"Naming Ceremony of Tianchu Aircraft," "Handover Ceremony of Yuehui Aircraft," "Aerobatic Performance of Aircraft Squadrons" - these large-character headlines stirred the curiosity of the broad masses in Shanghai. Cars, bicycles, rickshaws and pedestrians on the Hongqiao Road kicked up yellow dust for a time, thronging forward. I was one of them.

The weather that day was very spring-like, and people seemed to be in the mood for spring. The left half of the airfield, cordoned off, near the newly-built but unfinished hangars, was already a seething mass of heads. Fourteen aircraft were lined up in a row, with the Tianchu Zheng Aircraft, the fighter - fitted with machine guns - the Fu Aircraft, and the "Yuehui" and "Yuewen" aircraft placed in the centre, facing the temporary canopy of the auditorium.

Three o'clock struck, and at the sound of military music, the big shots on stage - those who donated the aircraft, those who received them, representatives of the government, officials from the Aeronautics Association, Aviation School, and Flying Club - proceeded to deliver the usual speeches. No loudspeakers had been set up on stage, and it could be safely said that what was being said could not be heard clearly beyond five paces. Fortunately, the audience's purpose was to see the aircraft display. The sensational speeches were left to the journalists to record.

The movement of the military band towards the aircraft bodies of the "Tianchu" indicated that the christening was about to begin. At this instant, a single spark on the northeast corner of the airfield suddenly began to burn across the winter-unmown reeds, and a southwest wind fanned it into a prairie fire. Armed police blew whistles and everyone threw their coats over it and tried to put it out. But the wind was strong and the grass was dry, and the flames snaked toward the northeast, forcing another group to quickly move the Eurasia Numbers 3 and 4 aircraft which had been parked there, narrowly averting disaster. Had there been fewer people, or had they been slower to act, several aircraft would have been offered to the "God of Fire" in moments! - The aromatic grass covering the airfield was simply a danger, a discarded cigarette end could turn into a bomb!

The propellers - the propellers - on the aircraft began to turn with a 地"地" [slow and heavy] sound, and the booming roar shocked the audience's eardrums, making the air tense. The "Yuewen" took off first, gracefully making several revolutions. Next came an aerobatic performance by the "Tianchu" fighter, which shot swiftly down and then surged 　, making several loops, to enthusiastic applause from the whole airfield. To conclude, the instructors from the aviation school, piloting the "Shanghai City", "Shanghai Business", "Shanghai Workers", "Shanghai School" and "Shanghai Boy Scouts" aircraft, flew in formation, circling the clouds. The yellow dust of the Hongqiao Road was stirred again by the cars of the returning audience speeding in single file.

Proverbs About Money 147

— Qifenglouzhu

It's not that I start writing about money for no reason, but in this snobbish modern society, everything depends on money. Since the ancient barter era, advancing to currency exchange, money has become the beginning of everything. No one can live without it for a day. If you have money, people will flock to you and welcome you, and your status will rise even if it's not high! If you don't have money, even if you are a 正直[righteous] gentleman, people will despise you! There is a world of difference between having money and not having money. A poet once wrote a poem about money, "With money, you can make ghosts turn the mill; without it, even brothers won't come." I have collected proverbs about money for your amusement.

Wealth should not be flaunted. Wealthy people are often weak. People die for wealth. You want money, not life. Wealth moves people's hearts. Look at the face of the copper coin. Wealth follows the wealthy. An ounce of gold is worth four ounces of fortune. People rely on copper coins, fish rely on water. Officials travel thousands of miles only for money. Having a thousand coins, you want ten thousand. Remember penniless days when you have money. Ill-gotten gains do not enrich the poor. As long as there are enough copper coins, you can carry a pagoda across the river. A hundred is wrong, a thousand is reasonable, ten thousand is foolproof. When poor, no one asks in the streets; when rich, even distant relatives visit in the deep mountains.

On a Night of Continuous Spring Rain 149

— Fu Jizhi

After drinking in the evening, I felt a little tired. I took a cigarette and lay horizontally on the oar to smoke. The smoke curled upwards and was blown out of the window by a slight breeze. It was probably still raining lightly. The water in the lead pipe was playing a long and clear tune. Outside the window was dark and沉沉 [gloomy]. On such a night of continuous spring rain, instead of saying it was宁静 [peaceful], it was better to say it was desolate, especially for me, with the mood of a romantic writer who had contracted "世纪病" (Malady of the Century), I felt endless emptiness and抑[depression]!

It was almost burning to my fingers, so I threw it on the ground. My body was still lazily unwilling to move. I was thinking: I felt that I should not have this decadent tendency, but should be active in the direction of interesting and meaningful life; although my so-called interesting and meaningful outlook on life seemed to have a color of personal hedonism.

On the surrounding mahogany bookshelves, there were gold-stamped, thread-bound, literary, and academic books. When I felt like reading, I would take out one or two and lie on the elastic sofa to browse, while smoking the cigarette I liked to smoke; before the rain, Sparrow's Tongue, I would always choose good tea to brew. Isn't this very carefree?

Outside the wall, under the weeping willows, was a clear and translucent shallow stream. When I was in a quiet mood, I would shake a painted boat to browse the miscellaneous trees and wildflowers standing along the shore; or I would let the boat flow with the water, and I would imitate that long-haired poet, squatting in the middle of the boat to pour wine and sing loudly. It seemed to be very meaningful, right?

If those sincere and unpretentious farmers were willing to chat with me, I could箕踞 [sit with legs spread out] on the green and oily field ridges to listen to them tell those缥渺 [vague] stories above Yi Huang; or I could sit alone under the peach forest and watch the gorgeous falling flowers flowing with the silent stream to that far and never-to-be-seen place; If not, I can also take my own Austin to the繁华𤍠闹 [bustling] city to live for three or five days, to change the air that is about to be bored, which is also a very self-enjoyable and rich-in-life meaning life!

However, the facts proved to me that this was completely an unattainable utopia. Wake up!

The water in the lead pipe was still flowing. The rain, at this time, thought it had not stopped.

European Tour 150

— Zhang Ruogu

㈢ The Carnival Festival in Nice

Nice is not only a famous scenic spot with pleasant weather for summering and wintering, but also a human paradise full of romance and joy. Every traveler who has participated in the Nice Carnival Festival cannot help but tirelessly praise the carnival fun enjoyed during the festival period upon returning.

Every year from July to September, while other places are experiencing the hot summer, Nice is always warm and bright like spring. Men and women with ample travel funds slip out from major European cities and come to Nice on the "Côte d'Azur" to spend a happy summer. The blue sea, the blue sky, the blue vehicles, the blue eyes, and the blue gemstone rings hold a grand exhibition on the golden beach.

In Nice, summer is always sunny and warm, without a single drop of rain. Travelers can leisurely enjoy the scenery and sunbathing. At dusk, a gentle breeze brings a feeling of tenderness everywhere. One can quietly sit alone on the Mediterranean coast and meditate, or climb the Alps with a lover, or browse novels under the shade of pine, cypress, and olive trees, or cheer and sing in a crowd of happy young men and women, what a free and unrestrained life!

In Nice, there are many festivals every year, which are days of joyful dancing and singing. In the summer of 1933, there were a total of three months of festival celebrations. Now, the names and dates of various festivals are copied below to show a glimpse of the grand occasion at that time. (July 2nd) Film Festival at the Mediterranean Palace, (9th) Children's Ball Game Day, (13th) Loie Fuller Dance at Albert I Park, (14th) French National Day street dancing and fireworks, (20th) International Air Travel Festival, (23rd) Motorcycle Race, (29th) Corso Blanc Night Ball, (30th) Maritime Games, (August 4th) International Alpine Car Race, (6th) Nice Car Race Day, (10th) to 27th, Bathing Suit Beauty Contest, (13th) Performance of famous dramas at the ancient theater ruins, (20th) to 23rd, French-Italian boxing competition, (27th) Football game, water polo game, (September 2nd) to 3rd Sea Dragon King Festival, (7th) American Bicycle Association, (10th) European Bicycle Race, (17th) Park Night Banquet, (24th) Grape Harvest Festival, city-wide parade and dance.

Every winter and spring, the Nice holidays are even more active than in summer. Now, according to the scheduled holiday calendar for 1934, the important programs are briefly listed as follows: (January 6th) Golf Game, (15th) to 21st Nice Tennis Championship, (20th) Royal Hotel Golf Game, (21st) Zishan Youzhuang Ball, (23rd) French Women's Red Cross Charity Performance, (27th) Legion of Honor Ball, (February 1st) Carnival Opening, (3rd) French Society for the Relief of Wounded Soldiers Ball (April Carnival Parade, (6th) Maritime Boat Race, Water Battle, (8th) Flower Throwing Festival, (8th) to 25th Nice 10th Market Exhibition, (10th) "Golden Grass" and "Red Stone" Ball, (11th) Public Dance, (12th) to 18th French Southern Tennis Championship, (13th) French Women's Day, (22nd) Flower Throwing Festival, (22nd) to 24th Golf Game, and Ice Skating Championship in this month. (March 2nd) "Nice Night" Grand Banquet Ball, (3rd) Golf Game, (8th) Flower Throwing Festival, (8th to 10th) Nice Golf Championship, (10th) White Ball, (11th) Dog Racing Festival, (12th) to 18th Lawn Tennis Championship, (21st) to 28th International Yacht Race, (25th) Children's Flower Throwing Festival, Pigeon Racing Festival, (31st) to April 4th French Provincial Celebration Festival, (April 1st) to 2nd International Air Race, (7th) to 11th Agricultural and Aquatic Products Exhibition, (8th) Nice Parade Festival, (16th) Sports Dance, (21st) French Officers Ball (30th) to May 6th "Côte d'Azur" Lawn Tennis Championship.

Among the holidays exemplified above, the "Carnival" is the most lively and interesting. The next time, the "Carnival" in Nice will be described in detail.
