Amateur Mailbox

Her Father Was So Angry He Hated Her 216

Editor:

There is a matter concerning my friend. Please reply immediately after receiving the letter in the Amateur Mailbox. Because I am about to leave Shanghai, and my friend's matter may change, please help me as much as possible. Not only will my friend be grateful, but I will also be very grateful. Sincerely, I wish you

Peace. Green Plum respectfully.

The matter asked about is written on the left:

My friend, Miss Wu, is studying at S Girls' School. She grew up in a very conservative aristocratic family. Last summer, a friend of her father acted as a matchmaker for her. It is said that the other party is very wealthy, but the family is very complicated, being a large family with concubines. Miss Wu, seeing that women often have unhappy marriages after marrying, wants to remain single. When her father told her that someone was proposing marriage for her, she opposed it, but her father ignored her and continued with the marriage. On the day the formal introduction was scheduled, Miss Wu suddenly fell ill and could not go. Her father was very angry. Later, with the persuasion of relatives, her father felt a little better and asked Wu if she was willing to get married. She replied, "I want to remain single." Her father said, "A woman who is single is not reliable, and who will she rely on after her parents die?" Her father absolutely would not let her go out to work, thinking it would be a loss of face, and told others: "No matter what, I will marry this daughter of mine off." However, Miss Wu strongly opposed it. At the time, her mother also did not approve of it, because the other party was a playboy and a hopelessly conservative family, so her mother did not want her daughter to suffer the hardship of being a daughter-in-law in such an old-fashioned family. Later, because of strong resistance, she actually rejected the marriage. But her father was very angry and from then on, he did not pay much attention to her, treating her worse than a stranger. Moreover, her father was often unwell because of this, and her father would get angry when he saw her. Miss Wu felt very uncomfortable seeing her father become like this. She thought, what is the point of living if she has lost the love of her dearest parents? Because of all kinds of worries, she regressed in her studies at school. However, her stubborn father still ignored her. She cried secretly every day, regretting that she should not have disobeyed her father's will. Her father wanted her to marry no matter what. If she obeyed her father's will, she really did not want to go to this family. Moreover, during the marriage process, there were all kinds of ominous omens. In addition, now that she has refused, there is no chance to salvage the situation. The mental pain she is currently in is indescribable. She also bears the guilt of being unfilial. She said: She sometimes hates so much that she would rather commit suicide, but she does not dare, because if she commits suicide, her family's relatives will gossip, especially since her family is a well-known family in society. So she is now destroying her own body, hoping to die early. But she still desperately hopes to regain her father's favor. After much thought, she decided: since her father insists that she marry, she might as well marry into the family that her father is satisfied with, and she can ignore all kinds of ominous omens. But she is a woman, how dare she say this? Moreover, the matchmaker is her father's friend, and she is not familiar with him. If she goes to ask him to re-propose this marriage, her father will know and will probably add fuel to the fire, and will be very angry—hating her for losing face. She is in this situation and really cannot solve her problem. She needs the high-minded Editor to give her a clear path. She does not hope for anything else now, only to gain her father's favor and a kind of mental comfort for herself, and she will be satisfied. Please teach her, sir.

Answer: Your friend, Miss Wu's father is so stubborn, such a person is truly unreasonable. However, your friend, in order to regain her father's favor, is willing to "ignore" herself and destroy herself. This filial piety is indeed admirable, but it is too unconcerned for herself. It is originally not impossible to sacrifice oneself for others, especially for one's dearest father, but we must first discuss whether it is worth sacrificing. We must do what is worthwhile and meaningful, and it is too foolish to do what is not worthwhile and meaningless. Marriage is originally one's own business, and whether the marriage is happy or not is also one's own business. Others can be said to have nothing to do with it, and originally have no right to interfere. Although China still retains the large family system, no one can approve of arranged marriages and not allow free love. Therefore, her opposition to her father arranging her marriage is a very proper thing. Her father hates her opposition and wants to throw a temper, but he is utterly confused, completely disregarding his daughter's feelings and her wishes. Therefore, the editor believes that she does not need to feel uneasy about her father's dissatisfaction and recognize herself as unfilial, let alone reluctantly submit to her own will and "marry into that family." Of course, within the possible range, she should also use various methods to hope to regain her father's favor. However, if other methods do not work and only this method will work, she still must not use this method. It must be known that disobeying one's father's will will certainly bear the "name of unfilial piety" and one's own heart will feel uneasy, but if one marries unhappily in the future and cannot get along with her husband or his family, the "mental pain" may still be "indescribable"! Life may still be meaningless!

In short, her father's anger is his own fault, and he is angry for no reason. As a child, there is no need to blindly follow his will. If he can put himself in his daughter's position and think from her point of view, he will probably regret that he should not have disobeyed his children's will. However, this is only our ideal. We should not have such expectations of him.

Finally, we believe that her one "clear path" is that she should have a change in her psychology in the future, that is, "decide her own affairs." She should seek employment, choose a spouse, and not worry about all kinds of vulgar face and things that people gossip about. Of course, this is not to persuade her to go her own way and be stubborn. We only hope that she can do things based on reason. Editor

Rain (Two) 218

— Zhang Yiping

"Ying Di, it's really you!" The visitor's tone was surprised, as if discovering a great secret.

That familiar voice and posture, I was embarrassed to hum and turn on the light next to the bed. The visitor smiled and watched me. I couldn't believe that my cousin Yuan Wen, who left without saying goodbye, was still as lively as she used to be.

"Wen Jie, what a surprise!"

"Surprise?" She turned around and sat on the edge of the desk.

I returned to my original position and offered her a cigarette. We exchanged glances, seemingly with nothing more to say. The sound of rain on the glass window was still as musical as before, but I no longer had the leisure to appreciate it. I busied myself tidying up.

"Ying Di, when did you come to Hangzhou?" She always said with a smile.

"Last winter," I replied faintly.

"It's been two years since we parted, right?" She looked up as if calculating. "I entered ×× school last summer, and I was so bored that I became the director of music. The weather was so good at noon today (I didn't expect it to rain now). I was dragged by some friends to visit the lake, and I ran into your colleagues at Yue Wang's tomb." She paused, giving a puzzling charming smile. "They always followed me and said frivolous things. In the end, they said that if Zhu Ying came today, even the lazybones would probably get excited."

"Ying Di, I really didn't expect you to come to Hangzhou!" She ended her self-narration with a smile.

Regarding this sudden visitor, Cousin Wen, perhaps because of our past disputes, I initially felt uneasy. But now, hearing her candid account of her intentions, during my day of troubles, I felt like I had found a friend and began to talk to her.

"Last autumn, I fell ill. I rented a small room, which was not convenient for recuperation, so I moved into the hospital." Speaking of this, I couldn't help but laugh. "Zhi Lin kept bothering me every day. I had no choice but to accept the advice of a friend and come here to teach English for twelve hours a week, partly to recuperate. After living here, I became too lazy to move."

"Lazybones, haha..." My cousin's attitude hadn't changed at all. She laughed honestly and unceremoniously. I reluctantly joined in the laughter. She suddenly asked me seriously:

"Ying Di, do you know who Zhi Lin married?"

I shook my head. I was really afraid to hear their names, but now, in an abnormal psychological state, I talked about it with someone I could talk to relatively easily. Instead, she seriously started talking about Zhi Lin. To prevent her from talking about anything else, I took out two cigarettes from the cigarette case, offered her one, lit them, and we started smoking.

"You might think it's an amazing story, Ying Di..." She made a dramatic pause, then leisurely started smoking. She seemed to be waiting for me to ask. However, I wasn't moved by her. At most, Zhi Lin's secret had been caught by her. Seeing that I didn't ask, she finally said, her attitude becoming even more serious, "She married Li Jian!"

She said it word by word, and I heard it word by word—She! Married! Li! Jian!!

Movie Special

Anecdotes and Witticisms of Eskimos in Hollywood (Part One) 219

— Guangdao

"Eskimo," which was shown at the Great Light Theater a few days ago, is a rare and excellent film that we have encountered in recent years. It can be said to be a widely acclaimed and universally praised blockbuster. I happened to see a passage about the interesting stories of these Eskimos in Hollywood in an old magazine. I found it very interesting, so I translated it to share with readers, hoping it won't feel like yesterday's news. However, before getting into the main text, we can first talk about the origin of these Eskimos and their living habits, etc.

Eskimos live in the far north of America, in Labrador, Greenland, Alaska, and other places in the Arctic. There are also such indigenous people in the far north of Asia, near the Bering Sea. The name "Eskimo" was originally given to them by the American Indians, and it means "people who eat raw meat." From this, we can know that the uncivilized indigenous red people of America are more knowledgeable and advanced than these Eskimos. As for what the Eskimos call themselves, it is Inuit, which means "the people." Because these people have been living in the extremely cold Arctic for tens of millions of years, their bodies cannot develop like those of temperate races, so they are very short. However, because they have to fight against the natural environment in order to survive, they are extremely strong. Therefore, the words "short but sturdy" are accurate to describe them. They rely entirely on fishing and hunting for a living all year round because there are no agricultural products. They eat meat raw, and when there is no fresh meat in winter, they take out the dried meat they have stored and gnaw on it, so their teeth are indeed amazing. After they hunt wild animals, they eat the meat and dry the skin to sew into clothes. They live in leather tents in the summer, and in circular caves made of stones or ice in the winter. There is a small hole for entering and exiting, which is narrow enough for only one person to pass through. About half of such houses are underground, partly to borrow some warmth from the ground, and partly to prevent the strong wind from blowing down the house. These people are probably of the Mongolian race, so their faces are very similar to those of us Asians, but their origins have not been determined by historians. Some say that they migrated from Northern Europe, but there are no traces of such people in Northern Europe.

In the film "Eskimo," in addition to the fishing and hunting scenes, blizzards, etc., which were filmed in the Arctic, a large part of it was also filmed in Hollywood. The director, Van Dyke, transported those actors from the icy and snowy land to sunny and hot California. The various inconveniences in their daily lives and their ignorance made them make many jokes. But at the same time, the simplicity and naturalness of their thoughts, and their inability to lie or flatter, gave the "civilized people" of Hollywood a thought-provoking criticism and advice. We can now record those things in a rambling manner.

When they arrived in Hollywood, just after getting off the train, there was a female star holding a German puppy in her arms. Camo Sook, who specializes in hunting walruses, saw it and laughed at Van Dyke; "How did that little walrus grow legs?" When they saw American women, they said, "American women are too pale; their bodies are too thin; they will freeze to death in the Arctic." Regarding food, they said, "The food is too bad. These things are too soft. It will ruin your teeth." Another person said, "There are too many sounds in your American places. Everything is too fast. Those gas-powered sleds run too fast on the street." Another person said, "There is too much sun here. The sun makes people's skin like that of a seal." (To be continued)

Audience Opinion

Review of "Spring Dreams of the Dance Hall" 220

— Xingqiao

The story of "Spring Dreams of the Dance Hall" is very ordinary, but its performance is extremely moving and can be said to be a successful work.

Set against the background of a dance hall, it depicts the suffering of dance girls, implying the evils of the city and the darkness of society. It grasps people's psychology, gives women today a hint of the path of life, makes the dance girls understand what kind of identity and life it is to be a dance girl, and gives a major lesson to the general dance girls of today. The meaning of the screenwriter is not bad.

The director's skills are still flexible, and there are few flaws in the overall picture. However, there is one place that may have been overlooked by the director, that is, when Zhao Yuquan impersonates Cai Xiaofeng and opens a room in the hotel upstairs in the dance hall. In the eyes of the audience, I am afraid that everyone thinks that Cai Xiaofeng is sick in the hospital, and will never come to the dance hall to open a room, and Li Manman will never believe this. Because the screen cannot show that Xiaofeng has recovered from his illness at this time, and the clothes and shoes that Manman is wearing were brought to her by the dance hall manager when she was taking care of Xiaofeng in the hospital, calling her to the dance hall. This is just like the first day she re-entered the dance hall. The screen does not show that Manman has been back in the dance hall for a while, and Xiaofeng's illness has also recovered, nor has she changed Manman's clothes and shoes to show that it has been many days: naturally, the audience will misunderstand. Those Who Can Unite Can Also Separate 221

— Fuxi

Is it the strange weather in Hollywood?

Hollywood is a special place for brewing romance.

This may be due to the weather. It may also be due to the influence of the film industry. But perhaps it is because those who make movies... those actors, directors, screenwriters, and producers... are mostly young, romantic, adventurous, and magnetic people. But whatever the force, it can brew and promote romance, and at the same time, it can equally break and destroy the established romance.

Taking the marriage of Alice White and Sidney Bartlett as an example, it can be said that it is the ultimate in pessimistic separation and reunion. Sidney Bartlett proposed to Alice White for five years. During this period, he suffered all kinds of sabotage, but the sabotage was not successful after all, and they held a grand wedding in Mexico. Alice was willing to give up her star status in order to marry Bartlett. She ignored the advice of the company and did not listen to the loyal advice of friends, just because she believed that Bartlett was the only lovable man among millions of people. Her unwavering love can also be admired by ordinary young men.

Alice's contract expired, and the company did not renew it with her. In this way, her star status was really ruined. But she was not willing to give in. She and Bartlett worked together to form a dance troupe and performed across the United States. Bartlett also did his best to help her rebuild her reputation. In this way, the couple struggled resolutely for a year and a half, and Alice White's name had become a household name. So one day they returned to Hollywood to restore her former status.

Alice's return to Hollywood caused a sensation, and she actually regained her star status—because she had signed a long-term contract with Universal. However, the weather in Hollywood or the film industry is to blame... Recently, it has been rumored that Alice White and Sidney Bartlett have disagreements. Alice often goes out with another man, and Bartlett often stays with another woman. It is said that they will be divorced soon.

Elliott Comes to China to Film a Yangtze River Movie 222

— Huang Yingdai

Hollywood producers have made many films in the past that insulted the Chinese people. Despite repeated opposition from the Chinese people, the attitude of the producers towards China remains the same. The problem of MGM's filming of "The Good Earth" has not yet been resolved, and now there is news that Clyde E. Elliott, a producer of horror films, will come to China to film a movie about the Yangtze River. Before their departure, the planned program was:

Exterior scenes: centered on the Yangtze River, with mountains, rivers, and rural areas as the backdrop. Subjects: Yangtze River floods, epidemics, pirates. Story: depicting the lives of farmers along the Yangtze River, and the floods of the Yangtze River, the prevalence of epidemics, and the rampant piracy. Actors: in addition to those they bring themselves, they hope to have five or six hundred Chinese people participate.

If the above-mentioned plan is true, then it is undoubtedly another film that insults the country. The purpose is nothing more than to point out the Chinese people's inability to prevent river floods, expose the farmers' ignorance of hygiene, leading to the prevalence of epidemics, and the rampant piracy everywhere, revealing the weakness of an unsettled society, which is very obvious. Regarding this issue, we hope that the government and the people of the country will pay attention to the state of its development. If this is true, we should naturally refuse to shoot it.

Elliott is a famous Hollywood director, known for filming travel horror films. He has been to South America and Africa to shoot many animal films, and "Bring 'Em Back Alive" and "Devil Tiger" are his two most successful films. The former had a special box office record when it was released, and the latter will be released soon.

It is said that the filming team has decided to set off in early April, so they expect to arrive in China during the Yangtze River floods. Elliott also believes that this period is also the time when piracy is most rampant along the Yangtze River. They will disregard all dangers and carry out filming work based on the above three points, floods, epidemics, and pirates, for a period of about six months. His wife and daughter will also come to China. I wonder how the Chinese authorities will respond to this news.

"Sports Queen"'s Morning Exercises 223

The day after filming the bathroom scene of "Sports Queen," director Sun Yu came up with another dormitory gimmick. When the sun poked its head out from the east mountain and opened its blood-red eyes to look into the dormitory of Jinghua School, countless healthy female athletes were lying on rows and rows of iron beds, performing morning exercises on the bed: exercising their arms and legs. Although they were all bare-chested and wore short shirts and underwear, director Sun's technique would never arouse any strange feelings. It could only make people feel that this was a serious and correct need, and perhaps make people feel ashamed of their own weakness. However, the conversation should turn around. Although this scenery is not sensual, it is very beautiful. The posture of the actors, the angle of the camera, the lighting facilities... are all very exquisite. When the arms and legs are raised together, row by row, in unison, or interwoven into various patterns, it is really heartening to see and unwilling to look away.

"Flames" Is Released, "Woman" Will Be Completed Soon 224

China's first film with fire as its backdrop, "Flames," was sent to Nanjing for inspection after it was completed. Because the quality and quantity were very sufficient, the inspection was quite satisfactory, and "Flames" was immediately approved.

The male lead of "Flames" is Peng Fei, a nationally renowned strongman, and the female lead is Hu Ping, who has considerable qualifications. Both of them have profound performances in the film, and the scene is magnificent, which is rare in domestic films. It has been decided that this film will be shown in the first-run theaters in Shanghai at the end of this month. Movie fans should pay attention to the huge advertisements in various newspapers these two days.

Here is another piece of news. Shi Dongshan's film "Woman" will be completed soon.

Movie Novel

Catherine the Great, Scarlet Empress (Ten) (One) 225

— Sumei

Catherine looked at his eyes, which seemed to be burning with the fire of love, but her attitude was as cold as ice. She said, "Please don't worry about me. Over the years, I have also understood what kind of person Russia needs from me, so I have also decided not to leave here." Alexei begged her, "Let me help you!" But Catherine shook her head and said, "I don't need your help. I will make my own decisions." After she finished speaking, she stretched out her hand for him to kiss and left him.

In the hall below, there was a sound of footsteps. Grand Duke Peter was leading a small team of soldiers and was walking over. They blocked Catherine's way. Peter suddenly ordered the soldiers, "Ready... aim..." He suddenly said to Catherine, as if he had not seen her just now, "Oh! Why didn't I see you... What a good target!" He then dismissed the soldiers first, and then walked up to Catherine and said in a low voice, "Come to my bedroom, I will introduce you to someone you don't know. He wants to live here for a long time." Catherine listened to him and ran to his bedroom without hesitation. There, she saw many toys everywhere. On a small piece of wood, there was a prototype of Catherine. The Grand Duke raised his knife and cut off its head with a wave. Peter laughed like a madman, "You don't know this kind of toy, I find it the most enjoyable." He then pulled open a small door, bowed, and Elizabeth came in. Catherine greeted her casually and said, "The Empress will be very happy if she hears that you are back." Peter said, "She won't know unless you tell her, but my advice to you is that it's better not to tell her." Catherine snorted and said, "I'll tell her? I can't even dream of doing it. She has her own group of secret detectives. And I won't interfere with what you like, as long as you don't interfere with my affairs." Elizabeth lifted her nose and said, "Let me tell you as soon as possible. When that old bat dies, Peter will marry me... Of course, the current Grand Duchess must be removed!" Catherine pretended not to hear Elizabeth's words and spun the horse-drawn carriage toy. She smiled at Peter and said, "Peter, are you still playing with this toy? You play with your toy, and I play with my toy." She said, and then walked away. Peter waited for Catherine to leave, then raised his knife and stabbed another Catherine prototype in the chest.

The Empress really died. The coffin was placed in the main hall, guarded by solemn soldiers on all sides. On the Empress's coffin sat a parrot and a monkey. Peter had already ascended the throne and was called the Tsar of All Russia. Flames of intrigue and counter-intrigue were fanned up on all sides of the palace. Catherine was inspecting the soldiers again, and bestowing many new favors on the young officers. The power holders of the state and the church held important meetings every day. One day Alexei came to secretly see Catherine again. He said, "Your Majesty, you are even more beautiful than ever." The Empress smiled. He said, "Do you really still like me that much?" (To be continued)
